Eliud begot Eleazar, Eleazar begot Matthan, and Matthan begot Jacob.
마태복음 : 1 장 16 절 
And Jacob begot Joseph the husband of Mary, of whom was born Jesus who is called Christ.
마태복음 : 1 장 17 절 
So all the generations from Abraham to David are fourteen generations, from David until the captivity in Babylon are fourteen generations, and from the captivity in Babylon until the Christ are fourteen generations.
마태복음 : 1 장 18 절 
Now the birth of Jesus Christ was as follows: After His mother Mary was betrothed to Joseph, before they came together, she was found with child of the Holy Spirit.
마태복음 : 1 장 19 절 
Then Joseph her husband, being a just man, and not wanting to make her a public example, was minded to put her away secretly.
마태복음 : 1 장 20 절 
But while he thought about these things, behold, an angel of the Lord appeared to him in a dream, saying, “Joseph, son of David, do not be afraid to take to you Mary your wife, for that which is conceived in her is of the Holy Spirit.
마태복음 : 1 장 21 절 
And she will bring forth a Son, and you shall call His name Jesus, for He will save His people from their sins.”
마태복음 : 1 장 22 절 
So all this was done that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the Lord through the prophet, saying:
마태복음 : 1 장 23 절 
“Behold, the virgin shall be with child, and bear a Son, and they shall call His name Immanuel,” which is translated, “God with us.”
마태복음 : 1 장 24 절 
Then Joseph, being aroused from sleep, did as the angel of the Lord commanded him and took to him his wife,
마태복음 : 1 장 25 절 
and did not know her till she had brought forth her firstborn Son. And he called His name Jesus.
마태복음 : 2 장 1 절 
Now after Jesus was born in Bethlehem of Judea in the days of Herod the king, behold, wise men from the East came to Jerusalem,
마태복음 : 2 장 2 절 
saying, “Where is He who has been born King of the Jews? For we have seen His star in the East and have come to worship Him.”
마태복음 : 2 장 3 절 
When Herod the king heard this, he was troubled, and all Jerusalem with him.
마태복음 : 2 장 4 절 
And when he had gathered all the chief priests and scribes of the people together, he inquired of them where the Christ was to be born.
마태복음 : 2 장 5 절 
So they said to him, “In Bethlehem of Judea, for thus it is written by the prophet:
마태복음 : 2 장 6 절 
‘But you, Bethlehem, in the land of Judah,
Are not the least among the rulers of Judah;
For out of you shall come a Ruler
Who will shepherd My people Israel.’ ”
마태복음 : 2 장 7 절 
Then Herod, when he had secretly called the wise men, determined from them what time the star appeared.
마태복음 : 2 장 8 절 
And he sent them to Bethlehem and said, “Go and search carefully for the young Child, and when you have found Him, bring back word to me, that I may come and worship Him also.”
마태복음 : 2 장 9 절 
When they heard the king, they departed; and behold, the star which they had seen in the East went before them, till it came and stood over where the young Child was.
마태복음 : 2 장 10 절 
When they saw the star, they rejoiced with exceedingly great joy.
마태복음 : 2 장 11 절 
And when they had come into the house, they saw the young Child with Mary His mother, and fell down and worshiped Him. And when they had opened their treasures, they presented gifts to Him: gold, frankincense, and myrrh.
마태복음 : 2 장 12 절 
Then, being divinely warned in a dream that they should not return to Herod, they departed for their own country another way.
마태복음 : 2 장 13 절 
Now when they had departed, behold, an angel of the Lord appeared to Joseph in a dream, saying, “Arise, take the young Child and His mother, flee to Egypt, and stay there until I bring you word; for Herod will seek the young Child to destroy Him.”
마태복음 : 2 장 14 절 
When he arose, he took the young Child and His mother by night and departed for Egypt,
마태복음 : 2 장 15 절 
and was there until the death of Herod, that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the Lord through the prophet, saying, “Out of Egypt I called My Son.”
마태복음 : 2 장 16 절 
Then Herod, when he saw that he was deceived by the wise men, was exceedingly angry; and he sent forth and put to death all the male children who were in Bethlehem and in all its districts, from two years old and under, according to the time which he had determined from the wise men.
마태복음 : 2 장 17 절 
Then was fulfilled what was spoken by Jeremiah the prophet, saying:
마태복음 : 2 장 18 절 
“A voice was heard in Ramah,
Lamentation, weeping, and great mourning,
Rachel weeping for her children,
Refusing to be comforted,
Because they are no more.”
마태복음 : 2 장 19 절 
Now when Herod was dead, behold, an angel of the Lord appeared in a dream to Joseph in Egypt,
마태복음 : 2 장 20 절 
saying, “Arise, take the young Child and His mother, and go to the land of Israel, for those who sought the young Child’s life are dead.”
마태복음 : 2 장 21 절 
Then he arose, took the young Child and His mother, and came into the land of Israel.
마태복음 : 2 장 22 절 
But when he heard that Archelaus was reigning over Judea instead of his father Herod, he was afraid to go there. And being warned by God in a dream, he turned aside into the region of Galilee.
마태복음 : 2 장 23 절 
And he came and dwelt in a city called Nazareth, that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the prophets, “He shall be called a Nazarene.”
마태복음 : 3 장 1 절 
In those days John the Baptist came preaching in the wilderness of Judea,
마태복음 : 3 장 2 절 
and saying, “Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand!”
마태복음 : 3 장 3 절 
For this is he who was spoken of by the prophet Isaiah, saying:
“The voice of one crying in the wilderness:
‘Prepare the way of the Lord;
Make His paths straight.’ ”
마태복음 : 3 장 4 절 
Now John himself was clothed in camel’s hair, with a leather belt around his waist; and his food was locusts and wild honey.
마태복음 : 3 장 5 절 
Then Jerusalem, all Judea, and all the region around the Jordan went out to him
마태복음 : 3 장 6 절 
and were baptized by him in the Jordan, confessing their sins.
마태복음 : 3 장 7 절 
But when he saw many of the Pharisees and Sadducees coming to his baptism, he said to them, “Brood of vipers! Who warned you to flee from the wrath to come?
마태복음 : 3 장 8 절 
Therefore bear fruits worthy of repentance,
마태복음 : 3 장 9 절 
and do not think to say to yourselves, ‘We have Abraham as our father.’ For I say to you that God is able to raise up children to Abraham from these stones.
마태복음 : 3 장 10 절 
And even now the ax is laid to the root of the trees. Therefore every tree which does not bear good fruit is cut down and thrown into the fire.
마태복음 : 3 장 11 절 
I indeed baptize you with water unto repentance, but He who is coming after me is mightier than I, whose sandals I am not worthy to carry. He will baptize you with the Holy Spirit and fire.
마태복음 : 3 장 12 절 
His winnowing fan is in His hand, and He will thoroughly clean out His threshing floor, and gather His wheat into the barn; but He will burn up the chaff with unquenchable fire.”
마태복음 : 3 장 13 절 
Then Jesus came from Galilee to John at the Jordan to be baptized by him.
마태복음 : 3 장 14 절 
And John tried to prevent Him, saying, “I need to be baptized by You, and are You coming to me?”
마태복음 : 3 장 15 절 
But Jesus answered and said to him, “Permit it to be so now, for thus it is fitting for us to fulfill all righteousness.” Then he allowed Him.
마태복음 : 3 장 16 절 
When He had been baptized, Jesus came up immediately from the water; and behold, the heavens were opened to Him, and He saw the Spirit of God descending like a dove and alighting upon Him.
마태복음 : 3 장 17 절 
And suddenly a voice came from heaven, saying, “This is My beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased.”
마태복음 : 4 장 1 절 
Then Jesus was led up by the Spirit into the wilderness to be tempted by the devil.
마태복음 : 4 장 2 절 
And when He had fasted forty days and forty nights, afterward He was hungry.
마태복음 : 4 장 3 절 
Now when the tempter came to Him, he said, “If You are the Son of God, command that these stones become bread.”
마태복음 : 4 장 4 절 
But He answered and said, “It is written, ‘Man shall not live by bread alone, but by every word that proceeds from the mouth of God.’”
마태복음 : 4 장 5 절 
Then the devil took Him up into the holy city, set Him on the pinnacle of the temple,
마태복음 : 4 장 6 절 
and said to Him, “If You are the Son of God, throw Yourself down. For it is written:
‘He shall give His angels charge over you,’
and,
In their hands they shall bear you up,
Lest you dash your foot against a stone.’ ”
마태복음 : 4 장 7 절 
Jesus said to him, “It is written again, ‘You shall not tempt the Lord your God.’ ”
마태복음 : 4 장 8 절 
Again, the devil took Him up on an exceedingly high mountain, and showed Him all the kingdoms of the world and their glory.
마태복음 : 4 장 9 절 
And he said to Him, “All these things I will give You if You will fall down and worship me.”
마태복음 : 4 장 10 절 
Then Jesus said to him, “Away with you, Satan! For it is written, ‘You shall worship the Lord your God, and Him only you shall serve.’ ”
마태복음 : 4 장 11 절 
Then the devil left Him, and behold, angels came and ministered to Him.
마태복음 : 4 장 12 절 
Now when Jesus heard that John had been put in prison, He departed to Galilee.
마태복음 : 4 장 13 절 
And leaving Nazareth, He came and dwelt in Capernaum, which is by the sea, in the regions of Zebulun and Naphtali,
마태복음 : 4 장 14 절 
that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by Isaiah the prophet, saying:
마태복음 : 4 장 15 절 
“The land of Zebulun and the land of Naphtali,
By the way of the sea, beyond the Jordan,
Galilee of the Gentiles:
마태복음 : 4 장 16 절 
The people who sat in darkness have seen a great light,
And upon those who sat in the region and shadow of death
Light has dawned.”
마태복음 : 4 장 17 절 
From that time Jesus began to preach and to say, “Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand.”
마태복음 : 4 장 18 절 
And Jesus, walking by the Sea of Galilee, saw two brothers, Simon called Peter, and Andrew his brother, casting a net into the sea; for they were fishermen.
마태복음 : 4 장 19 절 
Then He said to them, “Follow Me, and I will make you fishers of men.”
마태복음 : 4 장 20 절 
They immediately left their nets and followed Him.
마태복음 : 4 장 21 절 
Going on from there, He saw two other brothers, James the son of Zebedee, and John his brother, in the boat with Zebedee their father, mending their nets. He called them,
마태복음 : 4 장 22 절 
and immediately they left the boat and their father, and followed Him.
마태복음 : 4 장 23 절 
And Jesus went about all Galilee, teaching in their synagogues, preaching the gospel of the kingdom, and healing all kinds of sickness and all kinds of disease among the people.
마태복음 : 4 장 24 절 
Then His fame went throughout all Syria; and they brought to Him all sick people who were afflicted with various diseases and torments, and those who were demon-possessed, epileptics, and paralytics; and He healed them.
마태복음 : 4 장 25 절 
Great multitudes followed Him—from Galilee, and from Decapolis, Jerusalem, Judea, and beyond the Jordan.
마태복음 : 5 장 1 절 
And seeing the multitudes, He went up on a mountain, and when He was seated His disciples came to Him.
마태복음 : 5 장 2 절 
Then He opened His mouth and taught them, saying:
마태복음 : 5 장 3 절 
“Blessed are the poor in spirit,
For theirs is the kingdom of heaven.
마태복음 : 5 장 4 절 
Blessed are those who mourn,
For they shall be comforted.
마태복음 : 5 장 5 절 
Blessed are the meek,
For they shall inherit the earth.
마태복음 : 5 장 6 절 
Blessed are those who hunger and thirst for righteousness,
For they shall be filled.
마태복음 : 5 장 7 절 
Blessed are the merciful,
For they shall obtain mercy.
마태복음 : 5 장 8 절 
Blessed are the pure in heart,
For they shall see God.
마태복음 : 5 장 9 절 
Blessed are the peacemakers,
For they shall be called sons of God.
마태복음 : 5 장 10 절 
Blessed are those who are persecuted for righteousness’ sake,
For theirs is the kingdom of heaven.
마태복음 : 5 장 11 절 
“Blessed are you when they revile and persecute you, and say all kinds of evil against you falsely for My sake.
마태복음 : 5 장 12 절 
Rejoice and be exceedingly glad, for great is your reward in heaven, for so they persecuted the prophets who were before you.
마태복음 : 5 장 13 절 
“You are the salt of the earth; but if the salt loses its flavor, how shall it be seasoned? It is then good for nothing but to be thrown out and trampled underfoot by men.
마태복음 : 5 장 14 절 
“You are the light of the world. A city that is set on a hill cannot be hidden.
마태복음 : 5 장 15 절 
Nor do they light a lamp and put it under a basket, but on a lampstand, and it gives light to all who are in the house.
마태복음 : 5 장 16 절 
Let your light so shine before men, that they may see your good works and glorify your Father in heaven.
마태복음 : 5 장 17 절 
“Do not think that I came to destroy the Law or the Prophets. I did not come to destroy but to fulfill.
마태복음 : 5 장 18 절 
For assuredly, I say to you, till heaven and earth pass away, one jot or one  tittle will by no means pass from the law till all is fulfilled.
마태복음 : 5 장 19 절 
Whoever therefore breaks one of the least of these commandments, and teaches men so, shall be called least in the kingdom of heaven; but whoever does and teaches them, he shall be called great in the kingdom of heaven.
마태복음 : 5 장 20 절 
For I say to you, that unless your righteousness exceeds the righteousness of the scribes and Pharisees, you will by no means enter the kingdom of heaven.
마태복음 : 5 장 21 절 
“You have heard that it was said to those of old, ‘You shall not murder, and whoever murders will be in danger of the judgment.’
마태복음 : 5 장 22 절 
But I say to you that whoever is angry with his brother without a cause shall be in danger of the judgment. And whoever says to his brother, ‘Raca!’ shall be in danger of the council. But whoever says, ‘You fool!’ shall be in danger of hell fire.
마태복음 : 5 장 23 절 
Therefore if you bring your gift to the altar, and there remember that your brother has something against you,
마태복음 : 5 장 24 절 
leave your gift there before the altar, and go your way. First be reconciled to your brother, and then come and offer your gift.
마태복음 : 5 장 25 절 
Agree with your adversary quickly, while you are on the way with him, lest your adversary deliver you to the judge, the judge hand you over to the officer, and you be thrown into prison.
마태복음 : 5 장 26 절 
Assuredly, I say to you, you will by no means get out of there till you have paid the last penny.
마태복음 : 5 장 27 절 
“You have heard that it was said to those of old, ‘You shall not commit adultery.’
마태복음 : 5 장 28 절 
But I say to you that whoever looks at a woman to lust for her has already committed adultery with her in his heart.
마태복음 : 5 장 29 절 
If your right eye causes you to sin, pluck it out and cast it from you; for it is more profitable for you that one of your members perish, than for your whole body to be cast into hell.
마태복음 : 5 장 30 절 
And if your right hand causes you to sin, cut it off and cast it from you; for it is more profitable for you that one of your members perish, than for your whole body to be cast into hell.
마태복음 : 5 장 31 절 
“Furthermore it has been said, ‘Whoever divorces his wife, let him give her a certificate of divorce.’
마태복음 : 5 장 32 절 
But I say to you that whoever divorces his wife for any reason except sexual immorality causes her to commit adultery; and whoever marries a woman who is divorced commits adultery.
마태복음 : 5 장 33 절 
“Again you have heard that it was said to those of old, ‘You shall not swear falsely, but shall perform your oaths to the Lord.’
마태복음 : 5 장 34 절 
But I say to you, do not swear at all: neither by heaven, for it is God’s throne;
마태복음 : 5 장 35 절 
nor by the earth, for it is His footstool; nor by Jerusalem, for it is the city of the great King.
마태복음 : 5 장 36 절 
Nor shall you swear by your head, because you cannot make one hair white or black.
마태복음 : 5 장 37 절 
But let your ‘Yes’ be ‘Yes,’ and your ‘No,’ ‘No.’ For whatever is more than these is from the evil one.
마태복음 : 5 장 38 절 
“You have heard that it was said, ‘An eye for an eye and a tooth for a tooth.’
마태복음 : 5 장 39 절 
But I tell you not to resist an evil person. But whoever slaps you on your right cheek, turn the other to him also.
마태복음 : 5 장 40 절 
If anyone wants to sue you and take away your tunic, let him have your cloak also.
마태복음 : 5 장 41 절 
And whoever compels you to go one mile, go with him two.
마태복음 : 5 장 42 절 
Give to him who asks you, and from him who wants to borrow from you do not turn away.
마태복음 : 5 장 43 절 
“You have heard that it was said, ‘You shall love your neighbor and hate your enemy.’
마태복음 : 5 장 44 절 
But I say to you, love your enemies, bless those who curse you, do good to those who hate you, and pray for those who spitefully use you and persecute you,
마태복음 : 5 장 45 절 
that you may be sons of your Father in heaven; for He makes His sun rise on the evil and on the good, and sends rain on the just and on the unjust.
마태복음 : 5 장 46 절 
For if you love those who love you, what reward have you? Do not even the tax collectors do the same?
마태복음 : 5 장 47 절 
And if you greet your brethren only, what do you do more than others? Do not even the tax collectors do so?
마태복음 : 5 장 48 절 
Therefore you shall be perfect, just as your Father in heaven is perfect.
마태복음 : 6 장 1 절 
“Take heed that you do not do your charitable deeds before men, to be seen by them. Otherwise you have no reward from your Father in heaven.
마태복음 : 6 장 2 절 
Therefore, when you do a charitable deed, do not sound a trumpet before you as the hypocrites do in the synagogues and in the streets, that they may have glory from men. Assuredly, I say to you, they have their reward.
마태복음 : 6 장 3 절 
But when you do a charitable deed, do not let your left hand know what your right hand is doing,
마태복음 : 6 장 4 절 
that your charitable deed may be in secret; and your Father who sees in secret will Himself reward you openly.
마태복음 : 6 장 5 절 
“And when you pray, you shall not be like the hypocrites. For they love to pray standing in the synagogues and on the corners of the streets, that they may be seen by men. Assuredly, I say to you, they have their reward.
마태복음 : 6 장 6 절 
But you, when you pray, go into your room, and when you have shut your door, pray to your Father who is in the secret place; and your Father who sees in secret will reward you openly.
마태복음 : 6 장 7 절 
And when you pray, do not use vain repetitions as the heathen do. For they think that they will be heard for their many words.
마태복음 : 6 장 8 절 
“Therefore do not be like them. For your Father knows the things you have need of before you ask Him.
마태복음 : 6 장 9 절 
In this manner, therefore, pray:
Our Father in heaven,
Hallowed be Your name.
마태복음 : 6 장 10 절 
Your kingdom come.
Your will be done
On earth as it is in heaven.
마태복음 : 6 장 11 절 
Give us this day our daily bread.
마태복음 : 6 장 12 절 
And forgive us our debts,
As we forgive our debtors.
마태복음 : 6 장 13 절 
And do not lead us into temptation,
But deliver us from the evil one.
For Yours is the kingdom and the power and the glory forever. Amen.
마태복음 : 6 장 14 절 
“For if you forgive men their trespasses, your heavenly Father will also forgive you.
마태복음 : 6 장 15 절 
But if you do not forgive men their trespasses, neither will your Father forgive your trespasses.
마태복음 : 6 장 16 절 
“Moreover, when you fast, do not be like the hypocrites, with a sad countenance. For they disfigure their faces that they may appear to men to be fasting. Assuredly, I say to you, they have their reward.
마태복음 : 6 장 17 절 
But you, when you fast, anoint your head and wash your face,
마태복음 : 6 장 18 절 
so that you do not appear to men to be fasting, but to your Father who is in the secret place; and your Father who sees in secret will reward you openly.
마태복음 : 6 장 19 절 
“Do not lay up for yourselves treasures on earth, where moth and rust destroy and where thieves break in and steal;
마태복음 : 6 장 20 절 
but lay up for yourselves treasures in heaven, where neither moth nor rust destroys and where thieves do not break in and steal.
마태복음 : 6 장 21 절 
For where your treasure is, there your heart will be also.
마태복음 : 6 장 22 절 
 “The lamp of the body is the eye. If therefore your eye is good, your whole body will be full of light.
마태복음 : 6 장 23 절 
But if your eye is bad, your whole body will be full of darkness. If therefore the light that is in you is darkness, how great is that darkness!
마태복음 : 6 장 24 절 
“No one can serve two masters; for either he will hate the one and love the other, or else he will be loyal to the one and despise the other. You cannot serve God and mammon.
마태복음 : 6 장 25 절 
“Therefore I say to you, do not worry about your life, what you will eat or what you will drink; nor about your body, what you will put on. Is not life more than food and the body more than clothing?
마태복음 : 6 장 26 절 
Look at the birds of the air, for they neither sow nor reap nor gather into barns; yet your heavenly Father feeds them. Are you not of more value than they?
마태복음 : 6 장 27 절 
Which of you by worrying can add one cubit to his stature?
마태복음 : 6 장 28 절 
“So why do you worry about clothing? Consider the lilies of the field, how they grow: they neither toil nor spin;
마태복음 : 6 장 29 절 
and yet I say to you that even Solomon in all his glory was not arrayed like one of these.
마태복음 : 6 장 30 절 
Now if God so clothes the grass of the field, which today is, and tomorrow is thrown into the oven, will He not much more clothe you, O you of little faith?
마태복음 : 6 장 31 절 
“Therefore do not worry, saying, ‘What shall we eat?’ or ‘What shall we drink?’ or ‘What shall we wear?’
마태복음 : 6 장 32 절 
For after all these things the Gentiles seek. For your heavenly Father knows that you need all these things.
마태복음 : 6 장 33 절 
But seek first the kingdom of God and His righteousness, and all these things shall be added to you.
마태복음 : 6 장 34 절 
Therefore do not worry about tomorrow, for tomorrow will worry about its own things. Sufficient for the day is its own trouble.
마태복음 : 7 장 1 절 
“Judge not, that you be not judged.
마태복음 : 7 장 2 절 
For with what judgment you judge, you will be judged; and with the measure you use, it will be measured back to you.
마태복음 : 7 장 3 절 
And why do you look at the speck in your brother’s eye, but do not consider the plank in your own eye?
마태복음 : 7 장 4 절 
Or how can you say to your brother, ‘Let me remove the speck from your eye’; and look, a plank is in your own eye?
마태복음 : 7 장 5 절 
Hypocrite! First remove the plank from your own eye, and then you will see clearly to remove the speck from your brother’s eye.
마태복음 : 7 장 6 절 
“Do not give what is holy to the dogs; nor cast your pearls before swine, lest they trample them under their feet, and turn and tear you in pieces.
마태복음 : 7 장 7 절 
“Ask, and it will be given to you; seek, and you will find; knock, and it will be opened to you.
마태복음 : 7 장 8 절 
For everyone who asks receives, and he who seeks finds, and to him who knocks it will be opened.
마태복음 : 7 장 9 절 
Or what man is there among you who, if his son asks for bread, will give him a stone?
마태복음 : 7 장 10 절 
Or if he asks for a fish, will he give him a serpent?
마태복음 : 7 장 11 절 
If you then, being evil, know how to give good gifts to your children, how much more will your Father who is in heaven give good things to those who ask Him!
마태복음 : 7 장 12 절 
Therefore, whatever you want men to do to you, do also to them, for this is the Law and the Prophets.
마태복음 : 7 장 13 절 
“Enter by the narrow gate; for wide is the gate and broad is the way that leads to destruction, and there are many who go in by it.
마태복음 : 7 장 14 절 
Because narrow is the gate and difficult is the way which leads to life, and there are few who find it.
마태복음 : 7 장 15 절 
“Beware of false prophets, who come to you in sheep’s clothing, but inwardly they are ravenous wolves.
마태복음 : 7 장 16 절 
You will know them by their fruits. Do men gather grapes from thornbushes or figs from thistles?
마태복음 : 7 장 17 절 
Even so, every good tree bears good fruit, but a bad tree bears bad fruit.
마태복음 : 7 장 18 절 
A good tree cannot bear bad fruit, nor can a bad tree bear good fruit.
마태복음 : 7 장 19 절 
Every tree that does not bear good fruit is cut down and thrown into the fire.
마태복음 : 7 장 20 절 
Therefore by their fruits you will know them.
마태복음 : 7 장 21 절 
“Not everyone who says to Me, ‘Lord, Lord,’ shall enter the kingdom of heaven, but he who does the will of My Father in heaven.
마태복음 : 7 장 22 절 
Many will say to Me in that day, ‘Lord, Lord, have we not prophesied in Your name, cast out demons in Your name, and done many wonders in Your name?’
마태복음 : 7 장 23 절 
And then I will declare to them, ‘I never knew you; depart from Me, you who practice lawlessness!’
마태복음 : 7 장 24 절 
“Therefore whoever hears these sayings of Mine, and does them, I will liken him to a wise man who built his house on the rock:
마태복음 : 7 장 25 절 
and the rain descended, the floods came, and the winds blew and beat on that house; and it did not fall, for it was founded on the rock.
마태복음 : 7 장 26 절 
“But everyone who hears these sayings of Mine, and does not do them, will be like a foolish man who built his house on the sand:
마태복음 : 7 장 27 절 
and the rain descended, the floods came, and the winds blew and beat on that house; and it fell. And great was its fall.”
마태복음 : 7 장 28 절 
And so it was, when Jesus had ended these sayings, that the people were astonished at His teaching,
마태복음 : 7 장 29 절 
for He taught them as one having authority, and not as the scribes.
마태복음 : 8 장 1 절 
When He had come down from the mountain, great multitudes followed Him.
마태복음 : 8 장 2 절 
And behold, a leper came and worshiped Him, saying, “Lord, if You are willing, You can make me clean.”
마태복음 : 8 장 3 절 
Then Jesus put out His hand and touched him, saying, “I am willing; be cleansed.” Immediately his leprosy was cleansed.
마태복음 : 8 장 4 절 
And Jesus said to him, “See that you tell no one; but go your way, show yourself to the priest, and offer the gift that Moses commanded, as a testimony to them.”
마태복음 : 8 장 5 절 
Now when Jesus had entered Capernaum, a centurion came to Him, pleading with Him,
마태복음 : 8 장 6 절 
saying, “Lord, my servant is lying at home paralyzed, dreadfully tormented.”
마태복음 : 8 장 7 절 
And Jesus said to him, “I will come and heal him.”
마태복음 : 8 장 8 절 
The centurion answered and said, “Lord, I am not worthy that You should come under my roof. But only speak a word, and my servant will be healed.
마태복음 : 8 장 9 절 
For I also am a man under authority, having soldiers under me. And I say to this one, ‘Go,’ and he goes; and to another, ‘Come,’ and he comes; and to my servant, ‘Do this,’ and he does it.”
마태복음 : 8 장 10 절 
When Jesus heard it, He marveled, and said to those who followed, “Assuredly, I say to you, I have not found such great faith, not even in Israel!
마태복음 : 8 장 11 절 
And I say to you that many will come from east and west, and sit down with Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob in the kingdom of heaven.
마태복음 : 8 장 12 절 
But the sons of the kingdom will be cast out into outer darkness. There will be weeping and gnashing of teeth.”
마태복음 : 8 장 13 절 
Then Jesus said to the centurion, “Go your way; and as you have believed, so let it be done for you.” And his servant was healed that same hour.
마태복음 : 8 장 14 절 
Now when Jesus had come into Peter’s house, He saw his wife’s mother lying sick with a fever.
마태복음 : 8 장 15 절 
So He touched her hand, and the fever left her. And she arose and served them.
마태복음 : 8 장 16 절 
When evening had come, they brought to Him many who were demon-possessed. And He cast out the spirits with a word, and healed all who were sick,
마태복음 : 8 장 17 절 
that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by Isaiah the prophet, saying:
“He Himself took our infirmities
And bore our sicknesses.”
마태복음 : 8 장 18 절 
And when Jesus saw great multitudes about Him, He gave a command to depart to the other side.
마태복음 : 8 장 19 절 
Then a certain scribe came and said to Him, “Teacher, I will follow You wherever You go.”
마태복음 : 8 장 20 절 
And Jesus said to him, “Foxes have holes and birds of the air have nests, but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay His head.”
마태복음 : 8 장 21 절 
Then another of His disciples said to Him, “Lord, let me first go and bury my father.”
마태복음 : 8 장 22 절 
But Jesus said to him, “Follow Me, and let the dead bury their own dead.”
마태복음 : 8 장 23 절 
Now when He got into a boat, His disciples followed Him.
마태복음 : 8 장 24 절 
And suddenly a great tempest arose on the sea, so that the boat was covered with the waves. But He was asleep.
마태복음 : 8 장 25 절 
Then His disciples came to Him and awoke Him, saying, “Lord, save us! We are perishing!”
마태복음 : 8 장 26 절 
But He said to them, “Why are you fearful, O you of little faith?” Then He arose and rebuked the winds and the sea, and there was a great calm.
마태복음 : 8 장 27 절 
So the men marveled, saying, “Who can this be, that even the winds and the sea obey Him?”
마태복음 : 8 장 28 절 
When He had come to the other side, to the country of the Gergesenes, there met Him two demon-possessed men, coming out of the tombs, exceedingly fierce, so that no one could pass that way.
마태복음 : 8 장 29 절 
And suddenly they cried out, saying, “What have we to do with You, Jesus, You Son of God? Have You come here to torment us before the time?”
마태복음 : 8 장 30 절 
Now a good way off from them there was a herd of many swine feeding.
마태복음 : 8 장 31 절 
So the demons begged Him, saying, “If You cast us out, permit us to go away into the herd of swine.”
마태복음 : 8 장 32 절 
And He said to them, “Go.” So when they had come out, they went into the herd of swine. And suddenly the whole herd of swine ran violently down the steep place into the sea, and perished in the water.
마태복음 : 8 장 33 절 
Then those who kept them fled; and they went away into the city and told everything, including what had happened to the demon-possessed men.
마태복음 : 8 장 34 절 
And behold, the whole city came out to meet Jesus. And when they saw Him, they begged Him to depart from their region.
마태복음 : 9 장 1 절 
So He got into a boat, crossed over, and came to His own city.
마태복음 : 9 장 2 절 
Then behold, they brought to Him a paralytic lying on a bed. When Jesus saw their faith, He said to the paralytic, “Son, be of good cheer; your sins are forgiven you.”
마태복음 : 9 장 3 절 
And at once some of the scribes said within themselves, “This Man blasphemes!”
마태복음 : 9 장 4 절 
But Jesus, knowing their thoughts, said, “Why do you think evil in your hearts?
마태복음 : 9 장 5 절 
For which is easier, to say, ‘Your sins are forgiven you,’ or to say, ‘Arise and walk’?
마태복음 : 9 장 6 절 
But that you may know that the Son of Man has power on earth to forgive sins”—then He said to the paralytic, “Arise, take up your bed, and go to your house.”
마태복음 : 9 장 7 절 
And he arose and departed to his house.
마태복음 : 9 장 8 절 
Now when the multitudes saw it, they marveled and glorified God, who had given such power to men.
마태복음 : 9 장 9 절 
As Jesus passed on from there, He saw a man named Matthew sitting at the tax office. And He said to him, “Follow Me.” So he arose and followed Him.
마태복음 : 9 장 10 절 
Now it happened, as Jesus sat at the table in the house, that behold, many tax collectors and sinners came and sat down with Him and His disciples.
마태복음 : 9 장 11 절 
And when the Pharisees saw it, they said to His disciples, “Why does your Teacher eat with tax collectors and sinners?”
마태복음 : 9 장 12 절 
When Jesus heard that, He said to them, “Those who are well have no need of a physician, but those who are sick.
마태복음 : 9 장 13 절 
But go and learn what this means: ‘I desire mercy and not sacrifice.’ For I did not come to call the righteous, but sinners, to repentance.”
마태복음 : 9 장 14 절 
Then the disciples of John came to Him, saying, “Why do we and the Pharisees fast often, but Your disciples do not fast?”
마태복음 : 9 장 15 절 
And Jesus said to them, “Can the friends of the bridegroom mourn as long as the bridegroom is with them? But the days will come when the bridegroom will be taken away from them, and then they will fast.
마태복음 : 9 장 16 절 
No one puts a piece of unshrunk cloth on an old garment; for the patch pulls away from the garment, and the tear is made worse.
마태복음 : 9 장 17 절 
Nor do they put new wine into old wineskins, or else the wineskins break, the wine is spilled, and the wineskins are ruined. But they put new wine into new wineskins, and both are preserved.”
마태복음 : 9 장 18 절 
While He spoke these things to them, behold, a ruler came and worshiped Him, saying, “My daughter has just died, but come and lay Your hand on her and she will live.”
마태복음 : 9 장 19 절 
So Jesus arose and followed him, and so did His disciples.
마태복음 : 9 장 20 절 
And suddenly, a woman who had a flow of blood for twelve years came from behind and touched the hem of His garment.
마태복음 : 9 장 21 절 
For she said to herself, “If only I may touch His garment, I shall be made well.”
마태복음 : 9 장 22 절 
But Jesus turned around, and when He saw her He said, “Be of good cheer, daughter; your faith has made you well.” And the woman was made well from that hour.
마태복음 : 9 장 23 절 
When Jesus came into the ruler’s house, and saw the flute players and the noisy crowd wailing,
마태복음 : 9 장 24 절 
He said to them, “Make room, for the girl is not dead, but sleeping.” And they ridiculed Him.
마태복음 : 9 장 25 절 
But when the crowd was put outside, He went in and took her by the hand, and the girl arose.
마태복음 : 9 장 26 절 
And the report of this went out into all that land.
마태복음 : 9 장 27 절 
When Jesus departed from there, two blind men followed Him, crying out and saying, “Son of David, have mercy on us!”
마태복음 : 9 장 28 절 
And when He had come into the house, the blind men came to Him. And Jesus said to them, “Do you believe that I am able to do this?”
They said to Him, “Yes, Lord.”
마태복음 : 9 장 29 절 
Then He touched their eyes, saying, “According to your faith let it be to you.”
마태복음 : 9 장 30 절 
And their eyes were opened. And Jesus sternly warned them, saying, “See that no one knows it.”
마태복음 : 9 장 31 절 
But when they had departed, they spread the news about Him in all that country.
마태복음 : 9 장 32 절 
As they went out, behold, they brought to Him a man, mute and demon-possessed.
마태복음 : 9 장 33 절 
And when the demon was cast out, the mute spoke. And the multitudes marveled, saying, “It was never seen like this in Israel!”
마태복음 : 9 장 34 절 
But the Pharisees said, “He casts out demons by the ruler of the demons.”
마태복음 : 9 장 35 절 
Then Jesus went about all the cities and villages, teaching in their synagogues, preaching the gospel of the kingdom, and healing every sickness and every disease among the people.
마태복음 : 9 장 36 절 
But when He saw the multitudes, He was moved with compassion for them, because they were weary and scattered, like sheep having no shepherd.
마태복음 : 9 장 37 절 
Then He said to His disciples, “The harvest truly is plentiful, but the laborers are few.
마태복음 : 9 장 38 절 
Therefore pray the Lord of the harvest to send out laborers into His harvest.”
마태복음 : 10 장 1 절 
And when He had called His twelve disciples to Him, He gave them power over unclean spirits, to cast them out, and to heal all kinds of sickness and all kinds of disease.
마태복음 : 10 장 2 절 
Now the names of the twelve apostles are these: first, Simon, who is called Peter, and Andrew his brother; James the son of Zebedee, and John his brother;
마태복음 : 10 장 3 절 
Philip and Bartholomew; Thomas and Matthew the tax collector; James the son of Alphaeus, and Lebbaeus, whose surname was Thaddaeus;
마태복음 : 10 장 4 절 
Simon the Cananite, and Judas Iscariot, who also betrayed Him.
마태복음 : 10 장 5 절 
These twelve Jesus sent out and commanded them, saying: “Do not go into the way of the Gentiles, and do not enter a city of the Samaritans.
마태복음 : 10 장 6 절 
But go rather to the lost sheep of the house of Israel.
마태복음 : 10 장 7 절 
And as you go, preach, saying, ‘The kingdom of heaven is at hand.’
마태복음 : 10 장 8 절 
Heal the sick, cleanse the lepers, raise the dead, cast out demons. Freely you have received, freely give.
마태복음 : 10 장 9 절 
Provide neither gold nor silver nor copper in your money belts,
마태복음 : 10 장 10 절 
nor bag for your journey, nor two tunics, nor sandals, nor staffs; for a worker is worthy of his food.
마태복음 : 10 장 11 절 
“Now whatever city or town you enter, inquire who in it is worthy, and stay there till you go out.
마태복음 : 10 장 12 절 
And when you go into a household, greet it.
마태복음 : 10 장 13 절 
If the household is worthy, let your peace come upon it. But if it is not worthy, let your peace return to you.
마태복음 : 10 장 14 절 
And whoever will not receive you nor hear your words, when you depart from that house or city, shake off the dust from your feet.
마태복음 : 10 장 15 절 
Assuredly, I say to you, it will be more tolerable for the land of Sodom and Gomorrah in the day of judgment than for that city!
마태복음 : 10 장 16 절 
“Behold, I send you out as sheep in the midst of wolves. Therefore be wise as serpents and harmless as doves.
마태복음 : 10 장 17 절 
But beware of men, for they will deliver you up to councils and scourge you in their synagogues.
마태복음 : 10 장 18 절 
You will be brought before governors and kings for My sake, as a testimony to them and to the Gentiles.
마태복음 : 10 장 19 절 
But when they deliver you up, do not worry about how or what you should speak. For it will be given to you in that hour what you should speak;
마태복음 : 10 장 20 절 
for it is not you who speak, but the Spirit of your Father who speaks in you.
마태복음 : 10 장 21 절 
“Now brother will deliver up brother to death, and a father his child; and children will rise up against parents and cause them to be put to death.
마태복음 : 10 장 22 절 
And you will be hated by all for My name’s sake. But he who endures to the end will be saved.
마태복음 : 10 장 23 절 
When they persecute you in this city, flee to another. For assuredly, I say to you, you will not have gone through the cities of Israel before the Son of Man comes.
마태복음 : 10 장 24 절 
“A disciple is not above his teacher, nor a servant above his master.
마태복음 : 10 장 25 절 
It is enough for a disciple that he be like his teacher, and a servant like his master. If they have called the master of the house Beelzebub, how much more will they call those of his household!
마태복음 : 10 장 26 절 
Therefore do not fear them. For there is nothing covered that will not be revealed, and hidden that will not be known.
마태복음 : 10 장 27 절 
“Whatever I tell you in the dark, speak in the light; and what you hear in the ear, preach on the housetops.
마태복음 : 10 장 28 절 
And do not fear those who kill the body but cannot kill the soul. But rather fear Him who is able to destroy both soul and body in hell.
마태복음 : 10 장 29 절 
Are not two sparrows sold for a copper coin? And not one of them falls to the ground apart from your Father’s will.
마태복음 : 10 장 30 절 
But the very hairs of your head are all numbered.
마태복음 : 10 장 31 절 
Do not fear therefore; you are of more value than many sparrows.
마태복음 : 10 장 32 절 
“Therefore whoever confesses Me before men, him I will also confess before My Father who is in heaven.
마태복음 : 10 장 33 절 
But whoever denies Me before men, him I will also deny before My Father who is in heaven.
마태복음 : 10 장 34 절 
“Do not think that I came to bring peace on earth. I did not come to bring peace but a sword.
마태복음 : 10 장 35 절 
For I have come to ‘set a man against his father, a daughter against her mother, and a daughter-in-law against her mother-in-law’;
마태복음 : 10 장 36 절 
and ‘a man’s enemies will be those of his own household.’
마태복음 : 10 장 37 절 
He who loves father or mother more than Me is not worthy of Me. And he who loves son or daughter more than Me is not worthy of Me.
마태복음 : 10 장 38 절 
And he who does not take his cross and follow after Me is not worthy of Me.
마태복음 : 10 장 39 절 
He who finds his life will lose it, and he who loses his life for My sake will find it.
마태복음 : 10 장 40 절 
“He who receives you receives Me, and he who receives Me receives Him who sent Me.
마태복음 : 10 장 41 절 
He who receives a prophet in the name of a prophet shall receive a prophet’s reward. And he who receives a righteous man in the name of a righteous man shall receive a righteous man’s reward.
마태복음 : 10 장 42 절 
And whoever gives one of these little ones only a cup of cold water in the name of a disciple, assuredly, I say to you, he shall by no means lose his reward.”
마태복음 : 11 장 1 절 
Now it came to pass, when Jesus finished commanding His twelve disciples, that He departed from there to teach and to preach in their cities.
마태복음 : 11 장 2 절 
And when John had heard in prison about the works of Christ, he sent two of his disciples
마태복음 : 11 장 3 절 
and said to Him, “Are You the Coming One, or do we look for another?”
마태복음 : 11 장 4 절 
Jesus answered and said to them, “Go and tell John the things which you hear and see:
마태복음 : 11 장 5 절 
The blind see and the lame walk; the lepers are cleansed and the deaf hear; the dead are raised up and the poor have the gospel preached to them.
마태복음 : 11 장 6 절 
And blessed is he who is not offended because of Me.”
마태복음 : 11 장 7 절 
As they departed, Jesus began to say to the multitudes concerning John: “What did you go out into the wilderness to see? A reed shaken by the wind?
마태복음 : 11 장 8 절 
But what did you go out to see? A man clothed in soft garments? Indeed, those who wear soft clothing are in kings’ houses.
마태복음 : 11 장 9 절 
But what did you go out to see? A prophet? Yes, I say to you, and more than a prophet.
마태복음 : 11 장 10 절 
For this is he of whom it is written:
‘Behold, I send My messenger before Your face,
Who will prepare Your way before You.’
마태복음 : 11 장 11 절 
“Assuredly, I say to you, among those born of women there has not risen one greater than John the Baptist; but he who is least in the kingdom of heaven is greater than he.
마태복음 : 11 장 12 절 
And from the days of John the Baptist until now the kingdom of heaven suffers violence, and the violent take it by force.
마태복음 : 11 장 13 절 
For all the prophets and the law prophesied until John.
마태복음 : 11 장 14 절 
And if you are willing to receive it, he is Elijah who is to come.
마태복음 : 11 장 15 절 
He who has ears to hear, let him hear!
마태복음 : 11 장 16 절 
“But to what shall I liken this generation? It is like children sitting in the marketplaces and calling to their companions,
마태복음 : 11 장 17 절 
and saying:
‘We played the flute for you,
And you did not dance;
We mourned to you,
And you did not lament.’
마태복음 : 11 장 18 절 
For John came neither eating nor drinking, and they say, ‘He has a demon.’
마태복음 : 11 장 19 절 
The Son of Man came eating and drinking, and they say, ‘Look, a glutton and a winebibber, a friend of tax collectors and sinners!’ But wisdom is justified by her children.”
마태복음 : 11 장 20 절 
Then He began to rebuke the cities in which most of His mighty works had been done, because they did not repent:
마태복음 : 11 장 21 절 
“Woe to you, Chorazin! Woe to you, Bethsaida! For if the mighty works which were done in you had been done in Tyre and Sidon, they would have repented long ago in sackcloth and ashes.
마태복음 : 11 장 22 절 
But I say to you, it will be more tolerable for Tyre and Sidon in the day of judgment than for you.
마태복음 : 11 장 23 절 
And you, Capernaum, who are exalted to heaven, will be brought down to Hades; for if the mighty works which were done in you had been done in Sodom, it would have remained until this day.
마태복음 : 11 장 24 절 
But I say to you that it shall be more tolerable for the land of Sodom in the day of judgment than for you.”
마태복음 : 11 장 25 절 
At that time Jesus answered and said, “I thank You, Father, Lord of heaven and earth, that You have hidden these things from the wise and prudent and have revealed them to babes.
마태복음 : 11 장 26 절 
Even so, Father, for so it seemed good in Your sight.
마태복음 : 11 장 27 절 
All things have been delivered to Me by My Father, and no one knows the Son except the Father. Nor does anyone know the Father except the Son, and the one to whom the Son wills to reveal Him.
마태복음 : 11 장 28 절 
Come to Me, all you who labor and are heavy laden, and I will give you rest.
마태복음 : 11 장 29 절 
Take My yoke upon you and learn from Me, for I am gentle and lowly in heart, and you will find rest for your souls.
마태복음 : 11 장 30 절 
For My yoke is easy and My burden is light.”
마태복음 : 12 장 1 절 
At that time Jesus went through the grainfields on the Sabbath. And His disciples were hungry, and began to pluck heads of grain and to eat.
마태복음 : 12 장 2 절 
And when the Pharisees saw it, they said to Him, “Look, Your disciples are doing what is not lawful to do on the Sabbath!”
마태복음 : 12 장 3 절 
But He said to them, “Have you not read what David did when he was hungry, he and those who were with him:
마태복음 : 12 장 4 절 
how he entered the house of God and ate the showbread which was not lawful for him to eat, nor for those who were with him, but only for the priests?
마태복음 : 12 장 5 절 
Or have you not read in the law that on the Sabbath the priests in the temple profane the Sabbath, and are blameless?
마태복음 : 12 장 6 절 
Yet I say to you that in this place there is One greater than the temple.
마태복음 : 12 장 7 절 
But if you had known what this means, ‘I desire mercy and not sacrifice,’ you would not have condemned the guiltless.
마태복음 : 12 장 8 절 
For the Son of Man is Lord even of the Sabbath.”
마태복음 : 12 장 9 절 
Now when He had departed from there, He went into their synagogue.
마태복음 : 12 장 10 절 
And behold, there was a man who had a withered hand. And they asked Him, saying, “Is it lawful to heal on the Sabbath?”—that they might accuse Him.
마태복음 : 12 장 11 절 
Then He said to them, “What man is there among you who has one sheep, and if it falls into a pit on the Sabbath, will not lay hold of it and lift it out?
마태복음 : 12 장 12 절 
Of how much more value then is a man than a sheep? Therefore it is lawful to do good on the Sabbath.”
마태복음 : 12 장 13 절 
Then He said to the man, “Stretch out your hand.” And he stretched it out, and it was restored as whole as the other.
마태복음 : 12 장 14 절 
Then the Pharisees went out and plotted against Him, how they might destroy Him.
마태복음 : 12 장 15 절 
But when Jesus knew it, He withdrew from there. And great multitudes followed Him, and He healed them all.
마태복음 : 12 장 16 절 
Yet He warned them not to make Him known,
마태복음 : 12 장 17 절 
that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by Isaiah the prophet, saying:
마태복음 : 12 장 18 절 
“Behold! My Servant whom I have chosen,
My Beloved in whom My soul is well pleased!
I will put My Spirit upon Him,
And He will declare justice to the Gentiles.
마태복음 : 12 장 19 절 
He will not quarrel nor cry out,
Nor will anyone hear His voice in the streets.
마태복음 : 12 장 20 절 
A bruised reed He will not break,
And smoking flax He will not quench,
Till He sends forth justice to victory;
마태복음 : 12 장 21 절 
And in His name Gentiles will trust.”
마태복음 : 12 장 22 절 
Then one was brought to Him who was demon-possessed, blind and mute; and He healed him, so that the blind and mute man both spoke and saw.
마태복음 : 12 장 23 절 
And all the multitudes were amazed and said, “Could this be the Son of David?”
마태복음 : 12 장 24 절 
Now when the Pharisees heard it they said, “This fellow does not cast out demons except by Beelzebub, the ruler of the demons.”
마태복음 : 12 장 25 절 
But Jesus knew their thoughts, and said to them: “Every kingdom divided against itself is brought to desolation, and every city or house divided against itself will not stand.
마태복음 : 12 장 26 절 
If Satan casts out Satan, he is divided against himself. How then will his kingdom stand?
마태복음 : 12 장 27 절 
And if I cast out demons by Beelzebub, by whom do your sons cast them out? Therefore they shall be your judges.
마태복음 : 12 장 28 절 
But if I cast out demons by the Spirit of God, surely the kingdom of God has come upon you.
마태복음 : 12 장 29 절 
Or how can one enter a strong man’s house and plunder his goods, unless he first binds the strong man? And then he will plunder his house.
마태복음 : 12 장 30 절 
He who is not with Me is against Me, and he who does not gather with Me scatters abroad.
마태복음 : 12 장 31 절 
“Therefore I say to you, every sin and blasphemy will be forgiven men, but the blasphemy against the Spirit will not be forgiven men.
마태복음 : 12 장 32 절 
Anyone who speaks a word against the Son of Man, it will be forgiven him; but whoever speaks against the Holy Spirit, it will not be forgiven him, either in this age or in the age to come.
마태복음 : 12 장 33 절 
“Either make the tree good and its fruit good, or else make the tree bad and its fruit bad; for a tree is known by its fruit.
마태복음 : 12 장 34 절 
Brood of vipers! How can you, being evil, speak good things? For out of the abundance of the heart the mouth speaks.
마태복음 : 12 장 35 절 
A good man out of the good treasure of his heart brings forth good things, and an evil man out of the evil treasure brings forth evil things.
마태복음 : 12 장 36 절 
But I say to you that for every idle word men may speak, they will give account of it in the day of judgment.
마태복음 : 12 장 37 절 
For by your words you will be justified, and by your words you will be condemned.”
마태복음 : 12 장 38 절 
Then some of the scribes and Pharisees answered, saying, “Teacher, we want to see a sign from You.”
마태복음 : 12 장 39 절 
But He answered and said to them, “An evil and adulterous generation seeks after a sign, and no sign will be given to it except the sign of the prophet Jonah.
마태복음 : 12 장 40 절 
For as Jonah was three days and three nights in the belly of the great fish, so will the Son of Man be three days and three nights in the heart of the earth.
마태복음 : 12 장 41 절 
The men of Nineveh will rise up in the judgment with this generation and condemn it, because they repented at the preaching of Jonah; and indeed a greater than Jonah is here.
마태복음 : 12 장 42 절 
The queen of the South will rise up in the judgment with this generation and condemn it, for she came from the ends of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon; and indeed a greater than Solomon is here.
마태복음 : 12 장 43 절 
“When an unclean spirit goes out of a man, he goes through dry places, seeking rest, and finds none.
마태복음 : 12 장 44 절 
Then he says, ‘I will return to my house from which I came.’ And when he comes, he finds it empty, swept, and put in order.
마태복음 : 12 장 45 절 
Then he goes and takes with him seven other spirits more wicked than himself, and they enter and dwell there; and the last state of that man is worse than the first. So shall it also be with this wicked generation.”
마태복음 : 12 장 46 절 
While He was still talking to the multitudes, behold, His mother and brothers stood outside, seeking to speak with Him.
마태복음 : 12 장 47 절 
Then one said to Him, “Look, Your mother and Your brothers are standing outside, seeking to speak with You.”
마태복음 : 12 장 48 절 
But He answered and said to the one who told Him, “Who is My mother and who are My brothers?”
마태복음 : 12 장 49 절 
And He stretched out His hand toward His disciples and said, “Here are My mother and My brothers!
마태복음 : 12 장 50 절 
For whoever does the will of My Father in heaven is My brother and sister and mother.”
마태복음 : 13 장 1 절 
On the same day Jesus went out of the house and sat by the sea.
마태복음 : 13 장 2 절 
And great multitudes were gathered together to Him, so that He got into a boat and sat; and the whole multitude stood on the shore.
마태복음 : 13 장 3 절 
Then He spoke many things to them in parables, saying: “Behold, a sower went out to sow.
마태복음 : 13 장 4 절 
And as he sowed, some seed fell by the wayside; and the birds came and devoured them.
마태복음 : 13 장 5 절 
Some fell on stony places, where they did not have much earth; and they immediately sprang up because they had no depth of earth.
마태복음 : 13 장 6 절 
But when the sun was up they were scorched, and because they had no root they withered away.
마태복음 : 13 장 7 절 
And some fell among thorns, and the thorns sprang up and choked them.
마태복음 : 13 장 8 절 
But others fell on good ground and yielded a crop: some a hundredfold, some sixty, some thirty.
마태복음 : 13 장 9 절 
He who has ears to hear, let him hear!”
마태복음 : 13 장 10 절 
And the disciples came and said to Him, “Why do You speak to them in parables?”
마태복음 : 13 장 11 절 
He answered and said to them, “Because it has been given to you to know the mysteries of the kingdom of heaven, but to them it has not been given.
마태복음 : 13 장 12 절 
For whoever has, to him more will be given, and he will have abundance; but whoever does not have, even what he has will be taken away from him.
마태복음 : 13 장 13 절 
Therefore I speak to them in parables, because seeing they do not see, and hearing they do not hear, nor do they understand.
마태복음 : 13 장 14 절 
And in them the prophecy of Isaiah is fulfilled, which says:
‘Hearing you will hear and shall not understand,
And seeing you will see and not perceive;
마태복음 : 13 장 15 절 
For the hearts of this people have grown dull.
Their ears are hard of hearing,
And their eyes they have closed,
Lest they should see with their eyes and hear with their ears,
Lest they should understand with their hearts and turn,
So that I should heal them.’
마태복음 : 13 장 16 절 
But blessed are your eyes for they see, and your ears for they hear;
마태복음 : 13 장 17 절 
for assuredly, I say to you that many prophets and righteous men desired to see what you see, and did not see it, and to hear what you hear, and did not hear it.
마태복음 : 13 장 18 절 
“Therefore hear the parable of the sower:
마태복음 : 13 장 19 절 
When anyone hears the word of the kingdom, and does not understand it, then the wicked one comes and snatches away what was sown in his heart. This is he who received seed by the wayside.
마태복음 : 13 장 20 절 
But he who received the seed on stony places, this is he who hears the word and immediately receives it with joy;
마태복음 : 13 장 21 절 
yet he has no root in himself, but endures only for a while. For when tribulation or persecution arises because of the word, immediately he stumbles.
마태복음 : 13 장 22 절 
Now he who received seed among the thorns is he who hears the word, and the cares of this world and the deceitfulness of riches choke the word, and he becomes unfruitful.
마태복음 : 13 장 23 절 
But he who received seed on the good ground is he who hears the word and understands it, who indeed bears fruit and produces: some a hundredfold, some sixty, some thirty.”
마태복음 : 13 장 24 절 
Another parable He put forth to them, saying: “The kingdom of heaven is like a man who sowed good seed in his field;
마태복음 : 13 장 25 절 
but while men slept, his enemy came and sowed tares among the wheat and went his way.
마태복음 : 13 장 26 절 
But when the grain had sprouted and produced a crop, then the tares also appeared.
마태복음 : 13 장 27 절 
So the servants of the owner came and said to him, ‘Sir, did you not sow good seed in your field? How then does it have tares?’
마태복음 : 13 장 28 절 
He said to them, ‘An enemy has done this.’ The servants said to him, ‘Do you want us then to go and gather them up?’
마태복음 : 13 장 29 절 
But he said, ‘No, lest while you gather up the tares you also uproot the wheat with them.
마태복음 : 13 장 30 절 
Let both grow together until the harvest, and at the time of harvest I will say to the reapers, “First gather together the tares and bind them in bundles to burn them, but gather the wheat into my barn.” ’ ”
마태복음 : 13 장 31 절 
Another parable He put forth to them, saying: “The kingdom of heaven is like a mustard seed, which a man took and sowed in his field,
마태복음 : 13 장 32 절 
which indeed is the least of all the seeds; but when it is grown it is greater than the herbs and becomes a tree, so that the birds of the air come and nest in its branches.”
마태복음 : 13 장 33 절 
Another parable He spoke to them: “The kingdom of heaven is like leaven, which a woman took and hid in three measures of meal till it was all leavened.”
마태복음 : 13 장 34 절 
All these things Jesus spoke to the multitude in parables; and without a parable He did not speak to them,
마태복음 : 13 장 35 절 
that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the prophet, saying:
“I will open My mouth in parables;
I will utter things kept secret from the foundation of the world.”
마태복음 : 13 장 36 절 
Then Jesus sent the multitude away and went into the house. And His disciples came to Him, saying, “Explain to us the parable of the tares of the field.”
마태복음 : 13 장 37 절 
He answered and said to them: “He who sows the good seed is the Son of Man.
마태복음 : 13 장 38 절 
The field is the world, the good seeds are the sons of the kingdom, but the tares are the sons of the wicked one.
마태복음 : 13 장 39 절 
The enemy who sowed them is the devil, the harvest is the end of the age, and the reapers are the angels.
마태복음 : 13 장 40 절 
Therefore as the tares are gathered and burned in the fire, so it will be at the end of this age.
마태복음 : 13 장 41 절 
The Son of Man will send out His angels, and they will gather out of His kingdom all things that offend, and those who practice lawlessness,
마태복음 : 13 장 42 절 
and will cast them into the furnace of fire. There will be wailing and gnashing of teeth.
마태복음 : 13 장 43 절 
Then the righteous will shine forth as the sun in the kingdom of their Father. He who has ears to hear, let him hear!
마태복음 : 13 장 44 절 
“Again, the kingdom of heaven is like treasure hidden in a field, which a man found and hid; and for joy over it he goes and sells all that he has and buys that field.
마태복음 : 13 장 45 절 
“Again, the kingdom of heaven is like a merchant seeking beautiful pearls,
마태복음 : 13 장 46 절 
who, when he had found one pearl of great price, went and sold all that he had and bought it.
마태복음 : 13 장 47 절 
“Again, the kingdom of heaven is like a dragnet that was cast into the sea and gathered some of every kind,
마태복음 : 13 장 48 절 
which, when it was full, they drew to shore; and they sat down and gathered the good into vessels, but threw the bad away.
마태복음 : 13 장 49 절 
So it will be at the end of the age. The angels will come forth, separate the wicked from among the just,
마태복음 : 13 장 50 절 
and cast them into the furnace of fire. There will be wailing and gnashing of teeth.”
마태복음 : 13 장 51 절 
Jesus said to them, “Have you understood all these things?”
They said to Him, “Yes, Lord.”
마태복음 : 13 장 52 절 
Then He said to them, “Therefore every scribe instructed concerning the kingdom of heaven is like a householder who brings out of his treasure things new and old.”
마태복음 : 13 장 53 절 
Now it came to pass, when Jesus had finished these parables, that He departed from there.
마태복음 : 13 장 54 절 
When He had come to His own country, He taught them in their synagogue, so that they were astonished and said, “Where did this Man get this wisdom and these mighty works?
마태복음 : 13 장 55 절 
Is this not the carpenter’s son? Is not His mother called Mary? And His brothers James, Joses, Simon, and Judas?
마태복음 : 13 장 56 절 
And His sisters, are they not all with us? Where then did this Man get all these things?”
마태복음 : 13 장 57 절 
So they were offended at Him.
But Jesus said to them, “A prophet is not without honor except in his own country and in his own house.”
마태복음 : 13 장 58 절 
Now He did not do many mighty works there because of their unbelief.
마태복음 : 14 장 1 절 
At that time Herod the tetrarch heard the report about Jesus
마태복음 : 14 장 2 절 
and said to his servants, “This is John the Baptist; he is risen from the dead, and therefore these powers are at work in him.”
마태복음 : 14 장 3 절 
For Herod had laid hold of John and bound him, and put him in prison for the sake of Herodias, his brother Philip’s wife.
마태복음 : 14 장 4 절 
Because John had said to him, “It is not lawful for you to have her.”
마태복음 : 14 장 5 절 
And although he wanted to put him to death, he feared the multitude, because they counted him as a prophet.
마태복음 : 14 장 6 절 
But when Herod’s birthday was celebrated, the daughter of Herodias danced before them and pleased Herod.
마태복음 : 14 장 7 절 
Therefore he promised with an oath to give her whatever she might ask.
마태복음 : 14 장 8 절 
So she, having been prompted by her mother, said, “Give me John the Baptist’s head here on a platter.”
마태복음 : 14 장 9 절 
And the king was sorry; nevertheless, because of the oaths and because of those who sat with him, he commanded it to be given to her.
마태복음 : 14 장 10 절 
So he sent and had John beheaded in prison.
마태복음 : 14 장 11 절 
And his head was brought on a platter and given to the girl, and she brought it to her mother.
마태복음 : 14 장 12 절 
Then his disciples came and took away the body and buried it, and went and told Jesus.
마태복음 : 14 장 13 절 
When Jesus heard it, He departed from there by boat to a deserted place by Himself. But when the multitudes heard it, they followed Him on foot from the cities.
마태복음 : 14 장 14 절 
And when Jesus went out He saw a great multitude; and He was moved with compassion for them, and healed their sick.
마태복음 : 14 장 15 절 
When it was evening, His disciples came to Him, saying, “This is a deserted place, and the hour is already late. Send the multitudes away, that they may go into the villages and buy themselves food.”
마태복음 : 14 장 16 절 
But Jesus said to them, “They do not need to go away. You give them something to eat.”
마태복음 : 14 장 17 절 
And they said to Him, “We have here only five loaves and two fish.”
마태복음 : 14 장 18 절 
He said, “Bring them here to Me.”
마태복음 : 14 장 19 절 
Then He commanded the multitudes to sit down on the grass. And He took the five loaves and the two fish, and looking up to heaven, He blessed and broke and gave the loaves to the disciples; and the disciples gave to the multitudes.
마태복음 : 14 장 20 절 
So they all ate and were filled, and they took up twelve baskets full of the fragments that remained.
마태복음 : 14 장 21 절 
Now those who had eaten were about five thousand men, besides women and children.
마태복음 : 14 장 22 절 
Immediately Jesus made His disciples get into the boat and go before Him to the other side, while He sent the multitudes away.
마태복음 : 14 장 23 절 
And when He had sent the multitudes away, He went up on the mountain by Himself to pray. Now when evening came, He was alone there.
마태복음 : 14 장 24 절 
But the boat was now in the middle of the sea, tossed by the waves, for the wind was contrary.
마태복음 : 14 장 25 절 
Now in the fourth watch of the night Jesus went to them, walking on the sea.
마태복음 : 14 장 26 절 
And when the disciples saw Him walking on the sea, they were troubled, saying, “It is a ghost!” And they cried out for fear.
마태복음 : 14 장 27 절 
But immediately Jesus spoke to them, saying, “Be of good cheer! It is I; do not be afraid.”
마태복음 : 14 장 28 절 
And Peter answered Him and said, “Lord, if it is You, command me to come to You on the water.”
마태복음 : 14 장 29 절 
So He said, “Come.” And when Peter had come down out of the boat, he walked on the water to go to Jesus.
마태복음 : 14 장 30 절 
But when he saw that the wind was boisterous, he was afraid; and beginning to sink he cried out, saying, “Lord, save me!”
마태복음 : 14 장 31 절 
And immediately Jesus stretched out His hand and caught him, and said to him, “O you of little faith, why did you doubt?”
마태복음 : 14 장 32 절 
And when they got into the boat, the wind ceased.
마태복음 : 14 장 33 절 
Then those who were in the boat came and worshiped Him, saying, “Truly You are the Son of God.”
마태복음 : 14 장 34 절 
When they had crossed over, they came to the land of Gennesaret.
마태복음 : 14 장 35 절 
And when the men of that place recognized Him, they sent out into all that surrounding region, brought to Him all who were sick,
마태복음 : 14 장 36 절 
and begged Him that they might only touch the hem of His garment. And as many as touched it were made perfectly well.
마태복음 : 15 장 1 절 
Then the scribes and Pharisees who were from Jerusalem came to Jesus, saying,
마태복음 : 15 장 2 절 
“Why do Your disciples transgress the tradition of the elders? For they do not wash their hands when they eat bread.”
마태복음 : 15 장 3 절 
He answered and said to them, “Why do you also transgress the commandment of God because of your tradition?
마태복음 : 15 장 4 절 
For God commanded, saying, ‘Honor your father and your mother’; and, ‘He who curses father or mother, let him be put to death.’
마태복음 : 15 장 5 절 
But you say, ‘Whoever says to his father or mother, “Whatever profit you might have received from me is a gift to God”—
마태복음 : 15 장 6 절 
then he need not honor his father or mother.’ Thus you have made the commandment of God of no effect by your tradition.
마태복음 : 15 장 7 절 
Hypocrites! Well did Isaiah prophesy about you, saying:
마태복음 : 15 장 8 절 
‘These people draw near to Me with their mouth,
And honor Me with their lips,
But their heart is far from Me.
마태복음 : 15 장 9 절 
And in vain they worship Me,
Teaching as doctrines the commandments of men.’ ”
마태복음 : 15 장 10 절 
When He had called the multitude to Himself, He said to them, “Hear and understand:
마태복음 : 15 장 11 절 
Not what goes into the mouth defiles a man; but what comes out of the mouth, this defiles a man.”
마태복음 : 15 장 12 절 
Then His disciples came and said to Him, “Do You know that the Pharisees were offended when they heard this saying?”
마태복음 : 15 장 13 절 
But He answered and said, “Every plant which My heavenly Father has not planted will be uprooted.
마태복음 : 15 장 14 절 
Let them alone. They are blind leaders of the blind. And if the blind leads the blind, both will fall into a ditch.”
마태복음 : 15 장 15 절 
Then Peter answered and said to Him, “Explain this parable to us.”
마태복음 : 15 장 16 절 
So Jesus said, “Are you also still without understanding?
마태복음 : 15 장 17 절 
Do you not yet understand that whatever enters the mouth goes into the stomach and is eliminated?
마태복음 : 15 장 18 절 
But those things which proceed out of the mouth come from the heart, and they defile a man.
마태복음 : 15 장 19 절 
For out of the heart proceed evil thoughts, murders, adulteries, fornications, thefts, false witness, blasphemies.
마태복음 : 15 장 20 절 
These are the things which defile a man, but to eat with unwashed hands does not defile a man.”
마태복음 : 15 장 21 절 
Then Jesus went out from there and departed to the region of Tyre and Sidon.
마태복음 : 15 장 22 절 
And behold, a woman of Canaan came from that region and cried out to Him, saying, “Have mercy on me, O Lord, Son of David! My daughter is severely demon-possessed.”
마태복음 : 15 장 23 절 
But He answered her not a word.
And His disciples came and urged Him, saying, “Send her away, for she cries out after us.”
마태복음 : 15 장 24 절 
But He answered and said, “I was not sent except to the lost sheep of the house of Israel.”
마태복음 : 15 장 25 절 
Then she came and worshiped Him, saying, “Lord, help me!”
마태복음 : 15 장 26 절 
But He answered and said, “It is not good to take the children’s bread and throw it to the little dogs.”
마태복음 : 15 장 27 절 
And she said, “Yes, Lord, yet even the little dogs eat the crumbs which fall from their masters’ table.”
마태복음 : 15 장 28 절 
Then Jesus answered and said to her, “O woman, great is your faith! Let it be to you as you desire.” And her daughter was healed from that very hour.
마태복음 : 15 장 29 절 
Jesus departed from there, skirted the Sea of Galilee, and went up on the mountain and sat down there.
마태복음 : 15 장 30 절 
Then great multitudes came to Him, having with them the lame, blind, mute, maimed, and many others; and they laid them down at Jesus’ feet, and He healed them.
마태복음 : 15 장 31 절 
So the multitude marveled when they saw the mute speaking, the maimed made whole, the lame walking, and the blind seeing; and they glorified the God of Israel.
마태복음 : 15 장 32 절 
Now Jesus called His disciples to Himself and said, “I have compassion on the multitude, because they have now continued with Me three days and have nothing to eat. And I do not want to send them away hungry, lest they faint on the way.”
마태복음 : 15 장 33 절 
Then His disciples said to Him, “Where could we get enough bread in the wilderness to fill such a great multitude?”
마태복음 : 15 장 34 절 
Jesus said to them, “How many loaves do you have?”
And they said, “Seven, and a few little fish.”
마태복음 : 15 장 35 절 
So He commanded the multitude to sit down on the ground.
마태복음 : 15 장 36 절 
And He took the seven loaves and the fish and gave thanks, broke them and gave them to His disciples; and the disciples gave to the multitude.
마태복음 : 15 장 37 절 
So they all ate and were filled, and they took up seven large baskets full of the fragments that were left.
마태복음 : 15 장 38 절 
Now those who ate were four thousand men, besides women and children.
마태복음 : 15 장 39 절 
And He sent away the multitude, got into the boat, and came to the region of Magdala.
마태복음 : 16 장 1 절 
Then the Pharisees and Sadducees came, and testing Him asked that He would show them a sign from heaven.
마태복음 : 16 장 2 절 
He answered and said to them, “When it is evening you say, ‘It will be fair weather, for the sky is red’;
마태복음 : 16 장 3 절 
and in the morning, ‘It will be foul weather today, for the sky is red and threatening.’ Hypocrites! You know how to discern the face of the sky, but you cannot discern the signs of the times.
마태복음 : 16 장 4 절 
A wicked and adulterous generation seeks after a sign, and no sign shall be given to it except the sign of the prophet Jonah.” And He left them and departed.
마태복음 : 16 장 5 절 
Now when His disciples had come to the other side, they had forgotten to take bread.
마태복음 : 16 장 6 절 
Then Jesus said to them, “Take heed and beware of the leaven of the Pharisees and the Sadducees.”
마태복음 : 16 장 7 절 
And they reasoned among themselves, saying, “It is because we have taken no bread.”
마태복음 : 16 장 8 절 
But Jesus, being aware of it, said to them, “O you of little faith, why do you reason among yourselves because you have brought no bread?
마태복음 : 16 장 9 절 
Do you not yet understand, or remember the five loaves of the five thousand and how many baskets you took up?
마태복음 : 16 장 10 절 
Nor the seven loaves of the four thousand and how many large baskets you took up?
마태복음 : 16 장 11 절 
How is it you do not understand that I did not speak to you concerning bread?—but to beware of the leaven of the Pharisees and Sadducees.”
마태복음 : 16 장 12 절 
Then they understood that He did not tell them to beware of the leaven of bread, but of the doctrine of the Pharisees and Sadducees.
마태복음 : 16 장 13 절 
When Jesus came into the region of Caesarea Philippi, He asked His disciples, saying, “Who do men say that I, the Son of Man, am?”
마태복음 : 16 장 14 절 
So they said, “Some say John the Baptist, some Elijah, and others Jeremiah or one of the prophets.”
마태복음 : 16 장 15 절 
He said to them, “But who do you say that I am?”
마태복음 : 16 장 16 절 
Simon Peter answered and said, “You are the Christ, the Son of the living God.”
마태복음 : 16 장 17 절 
Jesus answered and said to him, “Blessed are you, Simon Bar-Jonah, for flesh and blood has not revealed this to you, but My Father who is in heaven.
마태복음 : 16 장 18 절 
And I also say to you that you are Peter, and on this rock I will build My church, and the gates of Hades shall not prevail against it.
마태복음 : 16 장 19 절 
And I will give you the keys of the kingdom of heaven, and whatever you bind on earth will be bound in heaven, and whatever you loose on earth will be loosed in heaven.”
마태복음 : 16 장 20 절 
Then He commanded His disciples that they should tell no one that He was Jesus the Christ.
마태복음 : 16 장 21 절 
From that time Jesus began to show to His disciples that He must go to Jerusalem, and suffer many things from the elders and chief priests and scribes, and be killed, and be raised the third day.
마태복음 : 16 장 22 절 
Then Peter took Him aside and began to rebuke Him, saying, “Far be it from You, Lord; this shall not happen to You!”
마태복음 : 16 장 23 절 
But He turned and said to Peter, “Get behind Me, Satan! You are an offense to Me, for you are not mindful of the things of God, but the things of men.”
마태복음 : 16 장 24 절 
Then Jesus said to His disciples, “If anyone desires to come after Me, let him deny himself, and take up his cross, and follow Me.
마태복음 : 16 장 25 절 
For whoever desires to save his life will lose it, but whoever loses his life for My sake will find it.
마태복음 : 16 장 26 절 
For what profit is it to a man if he gains the whole world, and loses his own soul? Or what will a man give in exchange for his soul?
마태복음 : 16 장 27 절 
For the Son of Man will come in the glory of His Father with His angels, and then He will reward each according to his works.
마태복음 : 16 장 28 절 
Assuredly, I say to you, there are some standing here who shall not taste death till they see the Son of Man coming in His kingdom.”
마태복음 : 17 장 1 절 
Now after six days Jesus took Peter, James, and John his brother, led them up on a high mountain by themselves;
마태복음 : 17 장 2 절 
and He was transfigured before them. His face shone like the sun, and His clothes became as white as the light.
마태복음 : 17 장 3 절 
And behold, Moses and Elijah appeared to them, talking with Him.
마태복음 : 17 장 4 절 
Then Peter answered and said to Jesus, “Lord, it is good for us to be here; if You wish, let us make here three tabernacles: one for You, one for Moses, and one for Elijah.”
마태복음 : 17 장 5 절 
While he was still speaking, behold, a bright cloud overshadowed them; and suddenly a voice came out of the cloud, saying, “This is My beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased. Hear Him!”
마태복음 : 17 장 6 절 
And when the disciples heard it, they fell on their faces and were greatly afraid.
마태복음 : 17 장 7 절 
But Jesus came and touched them and said, “Arise, and do not be afraid.”
마태복음 : 17 장 8 절 
When they had lifted up their eyes, they saw no one but Jesus only.
마태복음 : 17 장 9 절 
Now as they came down from the mountain, Jesus commanded them, saying, “Tell the vision to no one until the Son of Man is risen from the dead.”
마태복음 : 17 장 10 절 
And His disciples asked Him, saying, “Why then do the scribes say that Elijah must come first?”
마태복음 : 17 장 11 절 
Jesus answered and said to them, “Indeed, Elijah is coming first and will restore all things.
마태복음 : 17 장 12 절 
But I say to you that Elijah has come already, and they did not know him but did to him whatever they wished. Likewise the Son of Man is also about to suffer at their hands.”
마태복음 : 17 장 13 절 
Then the disciples understood that He spoke to them of John the Baptist.
마태복음 : 17 장 14 절 
And when they had come to the multitude, a man came to Him, kneeling down to Him and saying,
마태복음 : 17 장 15 절 
“Lord, have mercy on my son, for he is an epileptic and suffers severely; for he often falls into the fire and often into the water.
마태복음 : 17 장 16 절 
So I brought him to Your disciples, but they could not cure him.”
마태복음 : 17 장 17 절 
Then Jesus answered and said, “O faithless and perverse generation, how long shall I be with you? How long shall I bear with you? Bring him here to Me.”
마태복음 : 17 장 18 절 
And Jesus rebuked the demon, and it came out of him; and the child was cured from that very hour.
마태복음 : 17 장 19 절 
Then the disciples came to Jesus privately and said, “Why could we not cast it out?”
마태복음 : 17 장 20 절 
So Jesus said to them, “Because of your unbelief; for assuredly, I say to you, if you have faith as a mustard seed, you will say to this mountain, ‘Move from here to there,’ and it will move; and nothing will be impossible for you.
마태복음 : 17 장 21 절 
However, this kind does not go out except by prayer and fasting.”
마태복음 : 17 장 22 절 
Now while they were staying in Galilee, Jesus said to them, “The Son of Man is about to be betrayed into the hands of men,
마태복음 : 17 장 23 절 
and they will kill Him, and the third day He will be raised up.” And they were exceedingly sorrowful.
마태복음 : 17 장 24 절

마태복음 : 17 장 25 절 
He said, “Yes.”

마태복음 : 17 장 26 절 
Peter said to Him, “From strangers.”

마태복음 : 17 장 27 절 
Nevertheless, lest we offend them, go to the sea, cast in a hook, and take the fish that comes up first. And when you have opened its mouth, you will find a piece of money; take that and give it to them for Me and you.”
마태복음 : 18 장 1 절 
At that time the disciples came to Jesus, saying, “Who then is greatest in the kingdom of heaven?”
마태복음 : 18 장 2 절 
Then Jesus called a little child to Him, set him in the midst of them,
마태복음 : 18 장 3 절 
and said, “Assuredly, I say to you, unless you are converted and become as little children, you will by no means enter the kingdom of heaven.
마태복음 : 18 장 4 절 
Therefore whoever humbles himself as this little child is the greatest in the kingdom of heaven.
마태복음 : 18 장 5 절 
Whoever receives one little child like this in My name receives Me.
마태복음 : 18 장 6 절 
“Whoever causes one of these little ones who believe in Me to sin, it would be better for him if a millstone were hung around his neck, and he were drowned in the depth of the sea.
마태복음 : 18 장 7 절 
Woe to the world because of offenses! For offenses must come, but woe to that man by whom the offense comes!
마태복음 : 18 장 8 절 
“If your hand or foot causes you to sin, cut it off and cast it from you. It is better for you to enter into life lame or maimed, rather than having two hands or two feet, to be cast into the everlasting fire.
마태복음 : 18 장 9 절 
And if your eye causes you to sin, pluck it out and cast it from you. It is better for you to enter into life with one eye, rather than having two eyes, to be cast into hell fire.
마태복음 : 18 장 10 절 
“Take heed that you do not despise one of these little ones, for I say to you that in heaven their angels always see the face of My Father who is in heaven.
마태복음 : 18 장 11 절 
For the Son of Man has come to save that which was lost.
마태복음 : 18 장 12 절 
“What do you think? If a man has a hundred sheep, and one of them goes astray, does he not leave the ninety-nine and go to the mountains to seek the one that is straying?
마태복음 : 18 장 13 절 
And if he should find it, assuredly, I say to you, he rejoices more over that sheep than over the ninety-nine that did not go astray.
마태복음 : 18 장 14 절 
Even so it is not the will of your Father who is in heaven that one of these little ones should perish.
마태복음 : 18 장 15 절 
“Moreover if your brother sins against you, go and tell him his fault between you and him alone. If he hears you, you have gained your brother.
마태복음 : 18 장 16 절 
But if he will not hear, take with you one or two more, that ‘by the mouth of two or three witnesses every word may be established.’
마태복음 : 18 장 17 절 
And if he refuses to hear them, tell it to the church. But if he refuses even to hear the church, let him be to you like a heathen and a tax collector.
마태복음 : 18 장 18 절 
“Assuredly, I say to you, whatever you bind on earth will be bound in heaven, and whatever you loose on earth will be loosed in heaven.
마태복음 : 18 장 19 절 
“Again I say to you that if two of you agree on earth concerning anything that they ask, it will be done for them by My Father in heaven.
마태복음 : 18 장 20 절 
For where two or three are gathered together in My name, I am there in the midst of them.”
마태복음 : 18 장 21 절

마태복음 : 18 장 22 절 
Jesus said to him, “I do not say to you, up to seven times, but up to seventy times seven.
마태복음 : 18 장 23 절 
Therefore the kingdom of heaven is like a certain king who wanted to settle accounts with his servants.
마태복음 : 18 장 24 절 
And when he had begun to settle accounts, one was brought to him who owed him ten thousand talents.
마태복음 : 18 장 25 절 
But as he was not able to pay, his master commanded that he be sold, with his wife and children and all that he had, and that payment be made.
마태복음 : 18 장 26 절 
The servant therefore fell down before him, saying, ‘Master, have patience with me, and I will pay you all.’
마태복음 : 18 장 27 절 
Then the master of that servant was moved with compassion, released him, and forgave him the debt.
마태복음 : 18 장 28 절 
“But that servant went out and found one of his fellow servants who owed him a hundred denarii; and he laid hands on him and took him by the throat, saying, ‘Pay me what you owe!’
마태복음 : 18 장 29 절 
So his fellow servant fell down at his feet and begged him, saying, ‘Have patience with me, and I will pay you all.’
마태복음 : 18 장 30 절 
And he would not, but went and threw him into prison till he should pay the debt.
마태복음 : 18 장 31 절

마태복음 : 18 장 32 절 
Then his master, after he had called him, said to him, ‘You wicked servant! I forgave you all that debt because you begged me.
마태복음 : 18 장 33 절

마태복음 : 18 장 34 절 
And his master was angry, and delivered him to the torturers until he should pay all that was due to him.
마태복음 : 18 장 35 절 
“So My heavenly Father also will do to you if each of you, from his heart, does not forgive his brother his trespasses.”
마태복음 : 19 장 1 절

마태복음 : 19 장 2 절

마태복음 : 19 장 3 절

마태복음 : 19 장 4 절

마태복음 : 19 장 5 절

마태복음 : 19 장 6 절 
So then, they are no longer two but one flesh. Therefore what God has joined together, let not man separate.”
마태복음 : 19 장 7 절

마태복음 : 19 장 8 절

마태복음 : 19 장 9 절

마태복음 : 19 장 10 절

마태복음 : 19 장 11 절

마태복음 : 19 장 12 절
