마태복음 : 19 장 13 절

마태복음 : 19 장 14 절

마태복음 : 19 장 26 절

마태복음 : 19 장 30 절 
But many who are first will be last, and the last first.

마태복음 : 20 장 3 절

마태복음 : 20 장 4 절 
and said to them, ‘You also go into the vineyard, and whatever is right I will give you.’ So they went.
마태복음 : 20 장 5 절

마태복음 : 20 장 6 절

마태복음 : 20 장 7 절

마태복음 : 20 장 8 절

마태복음 : 20 장 9 절

마태복음 : 20 장 10 절

마태복음 : 20 장 12 절

마태복음 : 20 장 13 절

마태복음 : 20 장 29 절

마태복음 : 20 장 32 절

마태복음 : 20 장 34 절

saying to them, “Go into the village opposite you, and immediately you will find a donkey tied, and a colt with her. Loose them and bring them to Me.
마태복음 : 21 장 3 절

마태복음 : 21 장 4 절

‘Blessed is He who comes in the name of the Lord!’

마태복음 : 21 장 11 절

마태복음 : 21 장 16 절

마태복음 : 21 장 19 절

마태복음 : 21 장 20 절

마태복음 : 21 장 21 절

마태복음 : 21 장 22 절 
And whatever things you ask in prayer, believing, you will receive.”
마태복음 : 21 장 23 절

마태복음 : 21 장 24 절

마태복음 : 21 장 25 절

마태복음 : 21 장 26 절

마태복음 : 21 장 27 절

마태복음 : 21 장 28 절 
“But what do you think? A man had two sons, and he came to the first and said, ‘Son, go, work today in my vineyard.’
마태복음 : 21 장 29 절

마태복음 : 21 장 30 절

마태복음 : 21 장 31 절

마태복음 : 21 장 32 절

마태복음 : 21 장 33 절 
“Hear another parable: There was a certain landowner who planted a vineyard and set a hedge around it, dug a winepress in it and built a tower. And he leased it to vinedressers and went into a far country.
마태복음 : 21 장 34 절

마태복음 : 21 장 35 절

마태복음 : 21 장 36 절

마태복음 : 21 장 37 절 
Then last of all he sent his son to them, saying, ‘They will respect my son.’
마태복음 : 21 장 38 절 
But when the vinedressers saw the son, they said among themselves, ‘This is the heir. Come, let us kill him and seize his inheritance.’
마태복음 : 21 장 39 절 
So they took him and cast him out of the vineyard and killed him.
마태복음 : 21 장 40 절 
“Therefore, when the owner of the vineyard comes, what will he do to those vinedressers?”
마태복음 : 21 장 41 절 
They said to Him, “He will destroy those wicked men miserably, and lease his vineyard to other vinedressers who will render to him the fruits in their seasons.”
마태복음 : 21 장 42 절 
Jesus said to them, “Have you never read in the Scriptures:
‘The stone which the builders rejected
Has become the chief cornerstone.
This was the Lord’s doing,
And it is marvelous in our eyes’ ?
마태복음 : 21 장 43 절 
 “Therefore I say to you, the kingdom of God will be taken from you and given to a nation bearing the fruits of it.
마태복음 : 21 장 44 절 
And whoever falls on this stone will be broken; but on whomever it falls, it will grind him to powder.”
마태복음 : 21 장 45 절 
Now when the chief priests and Pharisees heard His parables, they perceived that He was speaking of them.
마태복음 : 21 장 46 절 
But when they sought to lay hands on Him, they feared the multitudes, because they took Him for a prophet.
마태복음 : 22 장 1 절 
And Jesus answered and spoke to them again by parables and said:
마태복음 : 22 장 2 절 
“The kingdom of heaven is like a certain king who arranged a marriage for his son,
마태복음 : 22 장 3 절 
and sent out his servants to call those who were invited to the wedding; and they were not willing to come.
마태복음 : 22 장 4 절 
Again, he sent out other servants, saying, ‘Tell those who are invited, “See, I have prepared my dinner; my oxen and fatted cattle are killed, and all things are ready. Come to the wedding.’ ”
마태복음 : 22 장 5 절 
But they made light of it and went their ways, one to his own farm, another to his business.
마태복음 : 22 장 6 절 
And the rest seized his servants, treated them spitefully, and killed them.
마태복음 : 22 장 7 절 
But when the king heard about it, he was furious. And he sent out his armies, destroyed those murderers, and burned up their city.
마태복음 : 22 장 8 절 
Then he said to his servants, ‘The wedding is ready, but those who were invited were not worthy.
마태복음 : 22 장 9 절 
Therefore go into the highways, and as many as you find, invite to the wedding.’
마태복음 : 22 장 10 절 
So those servants went out into the highways and gathered together all whom they found, both bad and good. And the wedding hall was filled with guests.
마태복음 : 22 장 11 절 
“But when the king came in to see the guests, he saw a man there who did not have on a wedding garment.
마태복음 : 22 장 12 절 
So he said to him, ‘Friend, how did you come in here without a wedding garment?’ And he was speechless.
마태복음 : 22 장 13 절 
Then the king said to the servants, ‘Bind him hand and foot, take him away, and cast him into outer darkness; there will be weeping and gnashing of teeth.’
마태복음 : 22 장 14 절 
“For many are called, but few are chosen.”
마태복음 : 22 장 15 절 
Then the Pharisees went and plotted how they might entangle Him in His talk.
마태복음 : 22 장 16 절 
And they sent to Him their disciples with the Herodians, saying, “Teacher, we know that You are true, and teach the way of God in truth; nor do You care about anyone, for You do not regard the person of men.
마태복음 : 22 장 17 절 
Tell us, therefore, what do You think? Is it lawful to pay taxes to Caesar, or not?”
마태복음 : 22 장 18 절 
But Jesus perceived their wickedness, and said, “Why do you test Me, you hypocrites?
마태복음 : 22 장 19 절 
Show Me the tax money.”
So they brought Him a denarius.
마태복음 : 22 장 20 절 
And He said to them, “Whose image and inscription is this?”
마태복음 : 22 장 21 절 
They said to Him, “Caesar’s.”
And He said to them, “Render therefore to Caesar the things that are Caesar’s, and to God the things that are God’s.” .
마태복음 : 22 장 22 절 
When they had heard these words, they marveled, and left Him and went their way.
마태복음 : 22 장 23 절 
The same day the Sadducees, who say there is no resurrection, came to Him and asked Him,
마태복음 : 22 장 24 절 
saying: “Teacher, Moses said that if a man dies, having no children, his brother shall marry his wife and raise up offspring for his brother.
마태복음 : 22 장 25 절 
Now there were with us seven brothers. The first died after he had married, and having no offspring, left his wife to his brother.
마태복음 : 22 장 26 절 
Likewise the second also, and the third, even to the seventh.
마태복음 : 22 장 27 절 
Last of all the woman died also.
마태복음 : 22 장 28 절 
Therefore, in the resurrection, whose wife of the seven will she be? For they all had her.”
마태복음 : 22 장 29 절 
Jesus answered and said to them, “You are mistaken, not knowing the Scriptures nor the power of God.
마태복음 : 22 장 30 절 
For in the resurrection they neither marry nor are given in marriage, but are like angels of God in heaven.
마태복음 : 22 장 31 절 
But concerning the resurrection of the dead, have you not read what was spoken to you by God, saying,
마태복음 : 22 장 32 절 
‘I am the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob’ ? God is not the God of the dead, but of the living.”
마태복음 : 22 장 33 절 
And when the multitudes heard this, they were astonished at His teaching.
마태복음 : 22 장 34 절 
But when the Pharisees heard that He had silenced the Sadducees, they gathered together.
마태복음 : 22 장 35 절 
Then one of them, a lawyer, asked Him a question, testing Him, and saying,
마태복음 : 22 장 36 절 
“Teacher, which is the great commandment in the law?”
마태복음 : 22 장 37 절 
Jesus said to him, ‘You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your mind.’
마태복음 : 22 장 38 절 
This is the first and great commandment.
마태복음 : 22 장 39 절 
And the second is like it: ‘You shall love your neighbor as yourself.’
마태복음 : 22 장 40 절 
On these two commandments hang all the Law and the Prophets.”
마태복음 : 22 장 41 절 
While the Pharisees were gathered together, Jesus asked them,
마태복음 : 22 장 42 절 
saying, “What do you think about the Christ? Whose Son is He?”
They said to Him, “The Son of David.”
마태복음 : 22 장 43 절 
He said to them, “How then does David in the Spirit call Him ‘Lord,’ saying:
마태복음 : 22 장 44 절 
‘The Lord said to my Lord,
“Sit at My right hand,
Till I make Your enemies Your footstool’ ”?
마태복음 : 22 장 45 절 
If David then calls Him ‘Lord,’ how is He his Son?”
마태복음 : 22 장 46 절 
And no one was able to answer Him a word, nor from that day on did anyone dare question Him anymore.
마태복음 : 23 장 1 절 
Then Jesus spoke to the multitudes and to His disciples,
마태복음 : 23 장 2 절 
saying: “The scribes and the Pharisees sit in Moses’ seat.
마태복음 : 23 장 3 절 
Therefore whatever they tell you to observe, that observe and do, but do not do according to their works; for they say, and do not do.
마태복음 : 23 장 4 절 
For they bind heavy burdens, hard to bear, and lay them on men’s shoulders; but they themselves will not move them with one of their fingers.
마태복음 : 23 장 5 절 
But all their works they do to be seen by men. They make their phylacteries broad and enlarge the borders of their garments.
마태복음 : 23 장 6 절 
They love the best places at feasts, the best seats in the synagogues,
마태복음 : 23 장 7 절 
greetings in the marketplaces, and to be called by men, ‘Rabbi, Rabbi.’
마태복음 : 23 장 8 절 
But you, do not be called ‘Rabbi’; for One is your Teacher, the Christ, and you are all brethren.
마태복음 : 23 장 9 절 
Do not call anyone on earth your father; for One is your Father, He who is in heaven.
마태복음 : 23 장 10 절 
And do not be called teachers; for One is your Teacher, the Christ.
마태복음 : 23 장 11 절 
But he who is greatest among you shall be your servant.
마태복음 : 23 장 12 절 
And whoever exalts himself will be humbled, and he who humbles himself will be exalted.
마태복음 : 23 장 13 절 
“But woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you shut up the kingdom of heaven against men; for you neither go in yourselves, nor do you allow those who are entering to go in.
마태복음 : 23 장 14 절 
Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you devour widows’ houses, and for a pretense make long prayers. Therefore you will receive greater condemnation.
마태복음 : 23 장 15 절 
“Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you travel land and sea to win one proselyte, and when he is won, you make him twice as much a son of hell as yourselves.
마태복음 : 23 장 16 절 
“Woe to you, blind guides, who say, ‘Whoever swears by the temple, it is nothing; but whoever swears by the gold of the temple, he is obliged to perform it.’
마태복음 : 23 장 17 절 
Fools and blind! For which is greater, the gold or the temple that sanctifies the gold?
마태복음 : 23 장 18 절 
And, ‘Whoever swears by the altar, it is nothing; but whoever swears by the gift that is on it, he is obliged to perform it.’
마태복음 : 23 장 19 절 
Fools and blind! For which is greater, the gift or the altar that sanctifies the gift?
마태복음 : 23 장 20 절 
Therefore he who swears by the altar, swears by it and by all things on it.
마태복음 : 23 장 21 절 
He who swears by the temple, swears by it and by Him who dwells in it.
마태복음 : 23 장 22 절 
And he who swears by heaven, swears by the throne of God and by Him who sits on it.
마태복음 : 23 장 23 절 
“Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you pay tithe of mint and anise and cummin, and have neglected the weightier matters of the law: justice and mercy and faith. These you ought to have done, without leaving the others undone.
마태복음 : 23 장 24 절 
Blind guides, who strain out a gnat and swallow a camel!
마태복음 : 23 장 25 절 
“Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you cleanse the outside of the cup and dish, but inside they are full of extortion and self-indulgence.
마태복음 : 23 장 26 절 
Blind Pharisee, first cleanse the inside of the cup and dish, that the outside of them may be clean also.
마태복음 : 23 장 27 절 
“Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you are like whitewashed tombs which indeed appear beautiful outwardly, but inside are full of dead men’s bones and all uncleanness.
마태복음 : 23 장 28 절 
Even so you also outwardly appear righteous to men, but inside you are full of hypocrisy and lawlessness.
마태복음 : 23 장 29 절 
“Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! Because you build the tombs of the prophets and adorn the monuments of the righteous,
마태복음 : 23 장 30 절 
and say, ‘If we had lived in the days of our fathers, we would not have been partakers with them in the blood of the prophets.’
마태복음 : 23 장 31 절 
“Therefore you are witnesses against yourselves that you are sons of those who murdered the prophets.
마태복음 : 23 장 32 절 
Fill up, then, the measure of your fathers’ guilt.
마태복음 : 23 장 33 절 
Serpents, brood of vipers! How can you escape the condemnation of hell?
마태복음 : 23 장 34 절 
Therefore, indeed, I send you prophets, wise men, and scribes: some of them you will kill and crucify, and some of them you will scourge in your synagogues and persecute from city to city,
마태복음 : 23 장 35 절 
that on you may come all the righteous blood shed on the earth, from the blood of righteous Abel to the blood of Zechariah, son of Berechiah, whom you murdered between the temple and the altar.
마태복음 : 23 장 36 절 
Assuredly, I say to you, all these things will come upon this generation.
마태복음 : 23 장 37 절 
“O Jerusalem, Jerusalem, the one who kills the prophets and stones those who are sent to her! How often I wanted to gather your children together, as a hen gathers her chicks under her wings, but you were not willing!
마태복음 : 23 장 38 절 
See! Your house is left to you desolate;
마태복음 : 23 장 39 절 
for I say to you, you shall see Me no more till you say, ‘Blessed is He who comes in the name of the Lord!’ ”
마태복음 : 24 장 1 절 
Then Jesus went out and departed from the temple, and His disciples came up to show Him the buildings of the temple.
마태복음 : 24 장 2 절 
And Jesus said to them, “Do you not see all these things? Assuredly, I say to you, not one stone shall be left here upon another, that shall not be thrown down.”
마태복음 : 24 장 3 절 
Now as He sat on the Mount of Olives, the disciples came to Him privately, saying, “Tell us, when will these things be? And what will be the sign of Your coming, and of the end of the age?”
마태복음 : 24 장 4 절 
And Jesus answered and said to them: “Take heed that no one deceives you.
마태복음 : 24 장 5 절 
For many will come in My name, saying, ‘I am the Christ,’ and will deceive many.
마태복음 : 24 장 6 절 
And you will hear of wars and rumors of wars. See that you are not troubled; for all these things must come to pass, but the end is not yet.
마태복음 : 24 장 7 절 
For nation will rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom. And there will be famines, pestilences, and earthquakes in various places.
마태복음 : 24 장 8 절 
All these are the beginning of sorrows.
마태복음 : 24 장 9 절 
“Then they will deliver you up to tribulation and kill you, and you will be hated by all nations for My name’s sake.
마태복음 : 24 장 10 절 
And then many will be offended, will betray one another, and will hate one another.
마태복음 : 24 장 11 절 
Then many false prophets will rise up and deceive many.
마태복음 : 24 장 12 절 
And because lawlessness will abound, the love of many will grow cold.
마태복음 : 24 장 13 절 
But he who endures to the end shall be saved.
마태복음 : 24 장 14 절 
And this gospel of the kingdom will be preached in all the world as a witness to all the nations, and then the end will come.
마태복음 : 24 장 15 절 
“Therefore when you see the ‘abomination of desolation,’ spoken of by Daniel the prophet, standing in the holy place” (whoever reads, let him understand),
마태복음 : 24 장 16 절 
“then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains.
마태복음 : 24 장 17 절 
Let him who is on the housetop not go down to take anything out of his house.
마태복음 : 24 장 18 절 
And let him who is in the field not go back to get his clothes.
마태복음 : 24 장 19 절 
But woe to those who are pregnant and to those who are nursing babies in those days!
마태복음 : 24 장 20 절 
And pray that your flight may not be in winter or on the Sabbath.
마태복음 : 24 장 21 절 
For then there will be great tribulation, such as has not been since the beginning of the world until this time, no, nor ever shall be.
마태복음 : 24 장 22 절 
And unless those days were shortened, no flesh would be saved; but for the elect’s sake those days will be shortened.
마태복음 : 24 장 23 절 
“Then if anyone says to you, ‘Look, here is the Christ!’ or ‘There!’ do not believe it.
마태복음 : 24 장 24 절 
For false christs and false prophets will rise and show great signs and wonders to deceive, if possible, even the elect.
마태복음 : 24 장 25 절 
See, I have told you beforehand.
마태복음 : 24 장 26 절 
“Therefore if they say to you, ‘Look, He is in the desert!’ do not go out; or ‘Look, He is in the inner rooms!’ do not believe it.
마태복음 : 24 장 27 절 
For as the lightning comes from the east and flashes to the west, so also will the coming of the Son of Man be.
마태복음 : 24 장 28 절 
For wherever the carcass is, there the eagles will be gathered together.
마태복음 : 24 장 29 절 
“Immediately after the tribulation of those days the sun will be darkened, and the moon will not give its light; the stars will fall from heaven, and the powers of the heavens will be shaken.
마태복음 : 24 장 30 절 
Then the sign of the Son of Man will appear in heaven, and then all the tribes of the earth will mourn, and they will see the Son of Man coming on the clouds of heaven with power and great glory.
마태복음 : 24 장 31 절 
And He will send His angels with a great sound of a trumpet, and they will gather together His elect from the four winds, from one end of heaven to the other.
마태복음 : 24 장 32 절 
“Now learn this parable from the fig tree: When its branch has already become tender and puts forth leaves, you know that summer is near.
마태복음 : 24 장 33 절 
So you also, when you see all these things, know that it is near—at the doors!
마태복음 : 24 장 34 절 
Assuredly, I say to you, this generation will by no means pass away till all these things take place.
마태복음 : 24 장 35 절 
Heaven and earth will pass away, but My words will by no means pass away.
마태복음 : 24 장 36 절 
“But of that day and hour no one knows, not even the angels of heaven, but My Father only.
마태복음 : 24 장 37 절 
But as the days of Noah were, so also will the coming of the Son of Man be.
마태복음 : 24 장 38 절 
For as in the days before the flood, they were eating and drinking, marrying and giving in marriage, until the day that Noah entered the ark,
마태복음 : 24 장 39 절 
and did not know until the flood came and took them all away, so also will the coming of the Son of Man be.
마태복음 : 24 장 40 절 
Then two men will be in the field: one will be taken and the other left.
마태복음 : 24 장 41 절 
Two women will be grinding at the mill: one will be taken and the other left.
마태복음 : 24 장 42 절 
Watch therefore, for you do not know what hour your Lord is coming.
마태복음 : 24 장 43 절 
But know this, that if the master of the house had known what hour the thief would come, he would have watched and not allowed his house to be broken into.
마태복음 : 24 장 44 절 
Therefore you also be ready, for the Son of Man is coming at an hour you do not expect.
마태복음 : 24 장 45 절 
“Who then is a faithful and wise servant, whom his master made ruler over his household, to give them food in due season?
마태복음 : 24 장 46 절 
Blessed is that servant whom his master, when he comes, will find so doing.
마태복음 : 24 장 47 절 
Assuredly, I say to you that he will make him ruler over all his goods.
마태복음 : 24 장 48 절 
But if that evil servant says in his heart, ‘My master is delaying his coming,’
마태복음 : 24 장 49 절 
and begins to beat his fellow servants, and to eat and drink with the drunkards,
마태복음 : 24 장 50 절 
the master of that servant will come on a day when he is not looking for him and at an hour that he is not aware of,
마태복음 : 24 장 51 절 
and will cut him in two and appoint him his portion with the hypocrites. There shall be weeping and gnashing of teeth.
마태복음 : 25 장 1 절 
“Then the kingdom of heaven shall be likened to ten virgins who took their lamps and went out to meet the bridegroom.
마태복음 : 25 장 2 절 
Now five of them were wise, and five were foolish.
마태복음 : 25 장 3 절 
Those who were foolish took their lamps and took no oil with them,
마태복음 : 25 장 4 절 
but the wise took oil in their vessels with their lamps.
마태복음 : 25 장 5 절 
But while the bridegroom was delayed, they all slumbered and slept.
마태복음 : 25 장 6 절 
“And at midnight a cry was heard: ‘Behold, the bridegroom is coming; go out to meet him!’
마태복음 : 25 장 7 절 
Then all those virgins arose and trimmed their lamps.
마태복음 : 25 장 8 절 
And the foolish said to the wise, ‘Give us some of your oil, for our lamps are going out.’
마태복음 : 25 장 9 절 
But the wise answered, saying, ‘No, lest there should not be enough for us and you; but go rather to those who sell, and buy for yourselves.’
마태복음 : 25 장 10 절 
And while they went to buy, the bridegroom came, and those who were ready went in with him to the wedding; and the door was shut.
마태복음 : 25 장 11 절 
“Afterward the other virgins came also, saying, ‘Lord, Lord, open to us!’
마태복음 : 25 장 12 절 
But he answered and said, ‘Assuredly, I say to you, I do not know you.’
마태복음 : 25 장 13 절 
“Watch therefore, for you know neither the day nor the hour in which the Son of Man is coming.
마태복음 : 25 장 14 절 
“For the kingdom of heaven is like a man traveling to a far country, who called his own servants and delivered his goods to them.
마태복음 : 25 장 15 절 
And to one he gave five talents, to another two, and to another one, to each according to his own ability; and immediately he went on a journey.
마태복음 : 25 장 16 절 
Then he who had received the five talents went and traded with them, and made another five talents.
마태복음 : 25 장 17 절 
And likewise he who had received two gained two more also.
마태복음 : 25 장 18 절 
But he who had received one went and dug in the ground, and hid his lord’s money.
마태복음 : 25 장 19 절 
After a long time the lord of those servants came and settled accounts with them.
마태복음 : 25 장 20 절 
“So he who had received five talents came and brought five other talents, saying, ‘Lord, you delivered to me five talents; look, I have gained five more talents besides them.’
마태복음 : 25 장 21 절 
His lord said to him, ‘Well done, good and faithful servant; you were faithful over a few things, I will make you ruler over many things. Enter into the joy of your lord.’
마태복음 : 25 장 22 절 
He also who had received two talents came and said, ‘Lord, you delivered to me two talents; look, I have gained two more talents besides them.’
마태복음 : 25 장 23 절 
His lord said to him, ‘Well done, good and faithful servant; you have been faithful over a few things, I will make you ruler over many things. Enter into the joy of your lord.’
마태복음 : 25 장 24 절 
“Then he who had received the one talent came and said, ‘Lord, I knew you to be a hard man, reaping where you have not sown, and gathering where you have not scattered seed.
마태복음 : 25 장 25 절 
And I was afraid, and went and hid your talent in the ground. Look, there you have what is yours.’
마태복음 : 25 장 26 절 
“But his lord answered and said to him, ‘You wicked and lazy servant, you knew that I reap where I have not sown, and gather where I have not scattered seed.
마태복음 : 25 장 27 절 
So you ought to have deposited my money with the bankers, and at my coming I would have received back my own with interest.
마태복음 : 25 장 28 절 
So take the talent from him, and give it to him who has ten talents.
마태복음 : 25 장 29 절 
‘For to everyone who has, more will be given, and he will have abundance; but from him who does not have, even what he has will be taken away.
마태복음 : 25 장 30 절 
And cast the unprofitable servant into the outer darkness. There will be weeping and gnashing of teeth.’
마태복음 : 25 장 31 절 
“When the Son of Man comes in His glory, and all the holy angels with Him, then He will sit on the throne of His glory.
마태복음 : 25 장 32 절 
All the nations will be gathered before Him, and He will separate them one from another, as a shepherd divides his sheep from the goats.
마태복음 : 25 장 33 절 
And He will set the sheep on His right hand, but the goats on the left.
마태복음 : 25 장 34 절 
Then the King will say to those on His right hand, ‘Come, you blessed of My Father, inherit the kingdom prepared for you from the foundation of the world:
마태복음 : 25 장 35 절 
for I was hungry and you gave Me food; I was thirsty and you gave Me drink; I was a stranger and you took Me in;
마태복음 : 25 장 36 절 
I was naked and you clothed Me; I was sick and you visited Me; I was in prison and you came to Me.’
마태복음 : 25 장 37 절 
“Then the righteous will answer Him, saying, ‘Lord, when did we see You hungry and feed You, or thirsty and give You drink?
마태복음 : 25 장 38 절 
When did we see You a stranger and take You in, or naked and clothe You?
마태복음 : 25 장 39 절 
Or when did we see You sick, or in prison, and come to You?’
마태복음 : 25 장 40 절 
And the King will answer and say to them, ‘Assuredly, I say to you, inasmuch as you did it to one of the least of these My brethren, you did it to Me.’
마태복음 : 25 장 41 절 
“Then He will also say to those on the left hand, ‘Depart from Me, you cursed, into the everlasting fire prepared for the devil and his angels:
마태복음 : 25 장 42 절 
for I was hungry and you gave Me no food; I was thirsty and you gave Me no drink;
마태복음 : 25 장 43 절 
I was a stranger and you did not take Me in, naked and you did not clothe Me, sick and in prison and you did not visit Me.’
마태복음 : 25 장 44 절 
“Then they also will answer Him, saying, ‘Lord, when did we see You hungry or thirsty or a stranger or naked or sick or in prison, and did not minister to You?’
마태복음 : 25 장 45 절 
Then He will answer them, saying, ‘Assuredly, I say to you, inasmuch as you did not do it to one of the least of these, you did not do it to Me.’
마태복음 : 25 장 46 절 
And these will go away into everlasting punishment, but the righteous into eternal life.”
마태복음 : 26 장 1 절 
Now it came to pass, when Jesus had finished all these sayings, that He said to His disciples,
마태복음 : 26 장 2 절 
“You know that after two days is the Passover, and the Son of Man will be delivered up to be crucified.”
마태복음 : 26 장 3 절 
Then the chief priests, the scribes, and the elders of the people assembled at the palace of the high priest, who was called Caiaphas,
마태복음 : 26 장 4 절 
and plotted to take Jesus by trickery and kill Him.
마태복음 : 26 장 5 절 
But they said, “Not during the feast, lest there be an uproar among the people.”
마태복음 : 26 장 6 절 
And when Jesus was in Bethany at the house of Simon the leper,
마태복음 : 26 장 7 절 
a woman came to Him having an alabaster flask of very costly fragrant oil, and she poured it on His head as He sat at the table.
마태복음 : 26 장 8 절 
But when His disciples saw it, they were indignant, saying, “Why this waste?
마태복음 : 26 장 9 절 
For this fragrant oil might have been sold for much and given to the poor.”
마태복음 : 26 장 10 절 
But when Jesus was aware of it, He said to them, “Why do you trouble the woman? For she has done a good work for Me.
마태복음 : 26 장 11 절 
For you have the poor with you always, but Me you do not have always.
마태복음 : 26 장 12 절 
For in pouring this fragrant oil on My body, she did it for My burial.
마태복음 : 26 장 13 절 
Assuredly, I say to you, wherever this gospel is preached in the whole world, what this woman has done will also be told as a memorial to her.”
마태복음 : 26 장 14 절 
Then one of the twelve, called Judas Iscariot, went to the chief priests
마태복음 : 26 장 15 절 
and said, “What are you willing to give me if I deliver Him to you?” And they counted out to him thirty pieces of silver.
마태복음 : 26 장 16 절 
So from that time he sought opportunity to betray Him.
마태복음 : 26 장 17 절 
Now on the first day of the Feast of Unleavened Bread the disciples came to Jesus, saying to Him, “Where do You want us to prepare for You to eat the Passover?”
마태복음 : 26 장 18 절 
And He said, “Go into the city to a certain man, and say to him, ‘The Teacher says, “My time is at hand; I will keep the Passover at your house with My disciples.” ’ ”
마태복음 : 26 장 19 절 
So the disciples did as Jesus had directed them; and they prepared the Passover.
마태복음 : 26 장 20 절 
When evening had come, He sat down with the twelve.
마태복음 : 26 장 21 절 
Now as they were eating, He said, “Assuredly, I say to you, one of you will betray Me.”
마태복음 : 26 장 22 절 
And they were exceedingly sorrowful, and each of them began to say to Him, “Lord, is it I?”
마태복음 : 26 장 23 절 
He answered and said, “He who dipped his hand with Me in the dish will betray Me.
마태복음 : 26 장 24 절 
The Son of Man indeed goes just as it is written of Him, but woe to that man by whom the Son of Man is betrayed! It would have been good for that man if he had not been born.”
마태복음 : 26 장 25 절 
Then Judas, who was betraying Him, answered and said, “Rabbi, is it I?”
He said to him, “You have said it.”
마태복음 : 26 장 26 절 
And as they were eating, Jesus took bread, blessed and broke it, and gave it to the disciples and said, “Take, eat; this is My body.”
마태복음 : 26 장 27 절 
Then He took the cup, and gave thanks, and gave it to them, saying, “Drink from it, all of you.
마태복음 : 26 장 28 절 
For this is My blood of the new covenant, which is shed for many for the remission of sins.
마태복음 : 26 장 29 절 
But I say to you, I will not drink of this fruit of the vine from now on until that day when I drink it new with you in My Father’s kingdom.”
마태복음 : 26 장 30 절 
And when they had sung a hymn, they went out to the Mount of Olives.
마태복음 : 26 장 31 절 
Then Jesus said to them, “All of you will be made to stumble because of Me this night, for it is written:
‘I will strike the Shepherd,
And the sheep of the flock will be scattered.’
마태복음 : 26 장 32 절 
But after I have been raised, I will go before you to Galilee.”
마태복음 : 26 장 33 절 
Peter answered and said to Him, “Even if all are made to stumble because of You, I will never be made to stumble.”
마태복음 : 26 장 34 절 
Jesus said to him, “Assuredly, I say to you that this night, before the rooster crows, you will deny Me three times.”
마태복음 : 26 장 35 절 
Peter said to Him, “Even if I have to die with You, I will not deny You!”
And so said all the disciples.
마태복음 : 26 장 36 절 
Then Jesus came with them to a place called Gethsemane, and said to the disciples, “Sit here while I go and pray over there.”
마태복음 : 26 장 37 절 
And He took with Him Peter and the two sons of Zebedee, and He began to be sorrowful and deeply distressed.
마태복음 : 26 장 38 절 
Then He said to them, “My soul is exceedingly sorrowful, even to death. Stay here and watch with Me.”
마태복음 : 26 장 39 절 
He went a little farther and fell on His face, and prayed, saying, “O My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from Me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as You will.”
마태복음 : 26 장 40 절 
Then He came to the disciples and found them sleeping, and said to Peter, “What! Could you not watch with Me one hour?
마태복음 : 26 장 41 절 
Watch and pray, lest you enter into temptation. The spirit indeed is willing, but the flesh is weak.”
마태복음 : 26 장 42 절 
Again, a second time, He went away and prayed, saying, “O My Father, if this cup cannot pass away from Me unless I drink it, Your will be done.”
마태복음 : 26 장 43 절 
And He came and found them asleep again, for their eyes were heavy.
마태복음 : 26 장 44 절 
So He left them, went away again, and prayed the third time, saying the same words.
마태복음 : 26 장 45 절 
Then He came to His disciples and said to them, “Are you still sleeping and resting? Behold, the hour is at hand, and the Son of Man is being betrayed into the hands of sinners.
마태복음 : 26 장 46 절 
Rise, let us be going. See, My betrayer is at hand.”
마태복음 : 26 장 47 절 
And while He was still speaking, behold, Judas, one of the twelve, with a great multitude with swords and clubs, came from the chief priests and elders of the people.
마태복음 : 26 장 48 절 
Now His betrayer had given them a sign, saying, “Whomever I kiss, He is the One; seize Him.”
마태복음 : 26 장 49 절 
Immediately he went up to Jesus and said, “Greetings, Rabbi!” and kissed Him.
마태복음 : 26 장 50 절 
But Jesus said to him, “Friend, why have you come?”
Then they came and laid hands on Jesus and took Him.
마태복음 : 26 장 51 절 
And suddenly, one of those who were with Jesus stretched out his hand and drew his sword, struck the servant of the high priest, and cut off his ear.
마태복음 : 26 장 52 절 
But Jesus said to him, “Put your sword in its place, for all who take the sword will perish by the sword.
마태복음 : 26 장 53 절 
Or do you think that I cannot now pray to My Father, and He will provide Me with more than twelve legions of angels?
마태복음 : 26 장 54 절 
How then could the Scriptures be fulfilled, that it must happen thus?”
마태복음 : 26 장 55 절 
In that hour Jesus said to the multitudes, “Have you come out, as against a robber, with swords and clubs to take Me? I sat daily with you, teaching in the temple, and you did not seize Me.
마태복음 : 26 장 56 절 
But all this was done that the Scriptures of the prophets might be fulfilled.”
Then all the disciples forsook Him and fled.
마태복음 : 26 장 57 절 
And those who had laid hold of Jesus led Him away to Caiaphas the high priest, where the scribes and the elders were assembled.
마태복음 : 26 장 58 절 
But Peter followed Him at a distance to the high priest’s courtyard. And he went in and sat with the servants to see the end.
마태복음 : 26 장 59 절 
Now the chief priests, the elders, and all the council sought false testimony against Jesus to put Him to death,
마태복음 : 26 장 60 절 
but found none. Even though many false witnesses came forward, they found none. But at last two false witnesses came forward
마태복음 : 26 장 61 절 
and said, “This fellow said, ‘I am able to destroy the temple of God and to build it in three days.’ ”
마태복음 : 26 장 62 절 
And the high priest arose and said to Him, “Do You answer nothing? What is it these men testify against You?”
마태복음 : 26 장 63 절 
But Jesus kept silent. And the high priest answered and said to Him, “I put You under oath by the living God: Tell us if You are the Christ, the Son of God!”
마태복음 : 26 장 64 절 
Jesus said to him, “It is as you said. Nevertheless, I say to you, hereafter you will see the Son of Man sitting at the right hand of the Power, and coming on the clouds of heaven.”
마태복음 : 26 장 65 절 
Then the high priest tore his clothes, saying, “He has spoken blasphemy! What further need do we have of witnesses? Look, now you have heard His blasphemy!
마태복음 : 26 장 66 절 
What do you think?”
They answered and said, “He is deserving of death.”
마태복음 : 26 장 67 절 
Then they spat in His face and beat Him; and others struck Him with the palms of their hands,
마태복음 : 26 장 68 절 
saying, “Prophesy to us, Christ! Who is the one who struck You?”
마태복음 : 26 장 69 절 
Now Peter sat outside in the courtyard. And a servant girl came to him, saying, “You also were with Jesus of Galilee.”
마태복음 : 26 장 70 절 
But he denied it before them all, saying, “I do not know what you are saying.”
마태복음 : 26 장 71 절 
And when he had gone out to the gateway, another girl saw him and said to those who were there, “This fellow also was with Jesus of Nazareth.”
마태복음 : 26 장 72 절 
But again he denied with an oath, “I do not know the Man!”
마태복음 : 26 장 73 절 
And a little later those who stood by came up and said to Peter, “Surely you also are one of them, for your speech betrays you.”
마태복음 : 26 장 74 절 
Then he began to curse and swear, saying, “I do not know the Man!”
Immediately a rooster crowed.
마태복음 : 26 장 75 절 
And Peter remembered the word of Jesus who had said to him, “Before the rooster crows, you will deny Me three times.” So he went out and wept bitterly.
마태복음 : 27 장 1 절 
When morning came, all the chief priests and elders of the people plotted against Jesus to put Him to death.
마태복음 : 27 장 2 절 
And when they had bound Him, they led Him away and delivered Him to Pontius Pilate the governor.
마태복음 : 27 장 3 절 
Then Judas, His betrayer, seeing that He had been condemned, was remorseful and brought back the thirty pieces of silver to the chief priests and elders,
마태복음 : 27 장 4 절 
saying, “I have sinned by betraying innocent blood.”
And they said, “What is that to us? You see to it!”
마태복음 : 27 장 5 절 
Then he threw down the pieces of silver in the temple and departed, and went and hanged himself.
마태복음 : 27 장 6 절 
But the chief priests took the silver pieces and said, “It is not lawful to put them into the treasury, because they are the price of blood.”
마태복음 : 27 장 7 절 
And they consulted together and bought with them the potter’s field, to bury strangers in.
마태복음 : 27 장 8 절 
Therefore that field has been called the Field of Blood to this day.
마태복음 : 27 장 9 절

마태복음 : 27 장 10 절 
and gave them for the potter’s field, as the Lord directed me.”
마태복음 : 27 장 11 절 
Now Jesus stood before the governor. And the governor asked Him, saying, “Are You the King of the Jews?”
Jesus said to him, “It is as you say.”
마태복음 : 27 장 12 절 
And while He was being accused by the chief priests and elders, He answered nothing.
마태복음 : 27 장 13 절 
Then Pilate said to Him, “Do You not hear how many things they testify against You?”
마태복음 : 27 장 14 절 
But He answered him not one word, so that the governor marveled greatly.
마태복음 : 27 장 15 절 
Now at the feast the governor was accustomed to releasing to the multitude one prisoner whom they wished.
마태복음 : 27 장 16 절 
And at that time they had a notorious prisoner called Barabbas.
마태복음 : 27 장 17 절 
Therefore, when they had gathered together, Pilate said to them, “Whom do you want me to release to you? Barabbas, or Jesus who is called Christ?”
마태복음 : 27 장 18 절 
For he knew that they had handed Him over because of envy.
마태복음 : 27 장 19 절 
While he was sitting on the judgment seat, his wife sent to him, saying, “Have nothing to do with that just Man, for I have suffered many things today in a dream because of Him.”
마태복음 : 27 장 20 절 
But the chief priests and elders persuaded the multitudes that they should ask for Barabbas and destroy Jesus.
마태복음 : 27 장 21 절 
The governor answered and said to them, “Which of the two do you want me to release to you?”
They said, “Barabbas!”
마태복음 : 27 장 22 절 
Pilate said to them, “What then shall I do with Jesus who is called Christ?”
They all said to him, “Let Him be crucified!”
마태복음 : 27 장 23 절 
Then the governor said, “Why, what evil has He done?”
But they cried out all the more, saying, “Let Him be crucified!”
마태복음 : 27 장 24 절 
When Pilate saw that he could not prevail at all, but rather that a tumult was rising, he took water and washed his hands before the multitude, saying, “I am innocent of the blood of this just Person. You see to it.”
마태복음 : 27 장 25 절 
And all the people answered and said, “His blood be on us and on our children.”
마태복음 : 27 장 26 절 
Then he released Barabbas to them; and when he had scourged Jesus, he delivered Him to be crucified.
마태복음 : 27 장 27 절 
Then the soldiers of the governor took Jesus into the Praetorium and gathered the whole garrison around Him.
마태복음 : 27 장 28 절 
And they stripped Him and put a scarlet robe on Him.
마태복음 : 27 장 29 절 
When they had twisted a crown of thorns, they put it on His head, and a reed in His right hand. And they bowed the knee before Him and mocked Him, saying, “Hail, King of the Jews!”
마태복음 : 27 장 30 절 
Then they spat on Him, and took the reed and struck Him on the head.
마태복음 : 27 장 31 절 
And when they had mocked Him, they took the robe off Him, put His own clothes on Him, and led Him away to be crucified.
마태복음 : 27 장 32 절 
Now as they came out, they found a man of Cyrene, Simon by name. Him they compelled to bear His cross.
마태복음 : 27 장 33 절 
And when they had come to a place called Golgotha, that is to say, Place of a Skull,
마태복음 : 27 장 34 절 
they gave Him sour wine mingled with gall to drink. But when He had tasted it, He would not drink.
마태복음 : 27 장 35 절 
Then they crucified Him, and divided His garments, casting lots, that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the prophet:
“They divided My garments among them,
And for My clothing they cast lots.”
마태복음 : 27 장 36 절 
Sitting down, they kept watch over Him there.
마태복음 : 27 장 37 절 
And they put up over His head the accusation written against Him:
THIS IS JESUS THE KING OF THE JEWS.
마태복음 : 27 장 38 절 
Then two robbers were crucified with Him, one on the right and another on the left.
마태복음 : 27 장 39 절 
And those who passed by blasphemed Him, wagging their heads
마태복음 : 27 장 40 절 
and saying, “You who destroy the temple and build it in three days, save Yourself! If You are the Son of God, come down from the cross.”
마태복음 : 27 장 41 절 
Likewise the chief priests also, mocking with the scribes and elders, said,
마태복음 : 27 장 42 절 
“He saved others; Himself He cannot save. If He is the King of Israel, let Him now come down from the cross, and we will believe Him.
마태복음 : 27 장 43 절 
He trusted in God; let Him deliver Him now if He will have Him; for He said, ‘I am the Son of God.’ ”
마태복음 : 27 장 44 절 
Even the robbers who were crucified with Him reviled Him with the same thing.
마태복음 : 27 장 45 절 
Now from the sixth hour until the ninth hour there was darkness over all the land.
마태복음 : 27 장 46 절 
And about the ninth hour Jesus cried out with a loud voice, saying, “Eli, Eli, lama sabachthani?” that is, “My God, My God, why have You forsaken Me?”
마태복음 : 27 장 47 절 
Some of those who stood there, when they heard that, said, “This Man is calling for Elijah!”
마태복음 : 27 장 48 절 
Immediately one of them ran and took a sponge, filled it with sour wine and put it on a reed, and offered it to Him to drink.
마태복음 : 27 장 49 절 
The rest said, “Let Him alone; let us see if Elijah will come to save Him.”
마태복음 : 27 장 50 절 
And Jesus cried out again with a loud voice, and yielded up His spirit.
마태복음 : 27 장 51 절 
Then, behold, the veil of the temple was torn in two from top to bottom; and the earth quaked, and the rocks were split,
마태복음 : 27 장 52 절 
and the graves were opened; and many bodies of the saints who had fallen asleep were raised;
마태복음 : 27 장 53 절 
and coming out of the graves after His resurrection, they went into the holy city and appeared to many.
마태복음 : 27 장 54 절

마태복음 : 27 장 55 절 
And many women who followed Jesus from Galilee, ministering to Him, were there looking on from afar,
마태복음 : 27 장 56 절 
among whom were Mary Magdalene, Mary the mother of James and Joses, and the mother of Zebedee’s sons.
마태복음 : 27 장 57 절 
Now when evening had come, there came a rich man from Arimathea, named Joseph, who himself had also become a disciple of Jesus.
마태복음 : 27 장 58 절 
This man went to Pilate and asked for the body of Jesus. Then Pilate commanded the body to be given to him.
마태복음 : 27 장 59 절 
When Joseph had taken the body, he wrapped it in a clean linen cloth,
마태복음 : 27 장 60 절 
and laid it in his new tomb which he had hewn out of the rock; and he rolled a large stone against the door of the tomb, and departed.
마태복음 : 27 장 61 절 
And Mary Magdalene was there, and the other Mary, sitting opposite the tomb.
마태복음 : 27 장 62 절 
On the next day, which followed the Day of Preparation, the chief priests and Pharisees gathered together to Pilate,
마태복음 : 27 장 63 절 
saying, “Sir, we remember, while He was still alive, how that deceiver said, ‘After three days I will rise.’
마태복음 : 27 장 64 절 
Therefore command that the tomb be made secure until the third day, lest His disciples come by night and steal Him away, and say to the people, ‘He has risen from the dead.’ So the last deception will be worse than the first.”
마태복음 : 27 장 65 절 
Pilate said to them, “You have a guard; go your way, make it as secure as you know how.”
마태복음 : 27 장 66 절 
So they went and made the tomb secure, sealing the stone and setting the guard.
마태복음 : 28 장 1 절 
Now after the Sabbath, as the first day of the week began to dawn, Mary Magdalene and the other Mary came to see the tomb.
마태복음 : 28 장 2 절 
And behold, there was a great earthquake; for an angel of the Lord descended from heaven, and came and rolled back the stone from the door, and sat on it.
마태복음 : 28 장 3 절 
His countenance was like lightning, and his clothing as white as snow.
마태복음 : 28 장 4 절 
And the guards shook for fear of him, and became like dead men.
마태복음 : 28 장 5 절 
But the angel answered and said to the women, “Do not be afraid, for I know that you seek Jesus who was crucified.
마태복음 : 28 장 6 절 
He is not here; for He is risen, as He said. Come, see the place where the Lord lay.
마태복음 : 28 장 7 절 
And go quickly and tell His disciples that He is risen from the dead, and indeed He is going before you into Galilee; there you will see Him. Behold, I have told you.”
마태복음 : 28 장 8 절 
So they went out quickly from the tomb with fear and great joy, and ran to bring His disciples word.
마태복음 : 28 장 9 절 
And as they went to tell His disciples, behold, Jesus met them, saying, “Rejoice!” So they came and held Him by the feet and worshiped Him.
마태복음 : 28 장 10 절 
Then Jesus said to them, “Do not be afraid. Go and tell My brethren to go to Galilee, and there they will see Me.”
마태복음 : 28 장 11 절 
Now while they were going, behold, some of the guard came into the city and reported to the chief priests all the things that had happened.
마태복음 : 28 장 12 절
