마태복음 : 19 장 22 절 
When the young man heard this, he went away sad, because he had great wealth.
마태복음 : 19 장 23 절 
Then Jesus said to his disciples, “Truly I tell you, it is hard for someone who is rich to enter the kingdom of heaven.
마태복음 : 19 장 24 절 
Again I tell you, it is easier for a camel to go through the eye of a needle than for someone who is rich to enter the kingdom of God.”
마태복음 : 19 장 25 절 
When the disciples heard this, they were greatly astonished and asked, “Who then can be saved?”
마태복음 : 19 장 26 절 
Jesus looked at them and said, “With man this is impossible, but with God all things are possible.”
마태복음 : 19 장 27 절 
Peter answered him, “We have left everything to follow you! What then will there be for us?”
마태복음 : 19 장 28 절

마태복음 : 19 장 29 절

마태복음 : 19 장 30 절 
But many who are first will be last, and many who are last will be first.
마태복음 : 20 장 1 절 
“For the kingdom of heaven is like a landowner who went out early in the morning to hire workers for his vineyard.
마태복음 : 20 장 2 절 
He agreed to pay them a denarius for the day and sent them into his vineyard.
마태복음 : 20 장 3 절 
“About nine in the morning he went out and saw others standing in the marketplace doing nothing.
마태복음 : 20 장 4 절 
He told them, ‘You also go and work in my vineyard, and I will pay you whatever is right.’
마태복음 : 20 장 5 절 
So they went.
“He went out again about noon and about three in the afternoon and did the same thing.
마태복음 : 20 장 6 절 
About five in the afternoon he went out and found still others standing around. He asked them, ‘Why have you been standing here all day long doing nothing?’
마태복음 : 20 장 7 절 
“ ‘Because no one has hired us,’ they answered.
“He said to them, ‘You also go and work in my vineyard.’
마태복음 : 20 장 8 절 
“When evening came, the owner of the vineyard said to his foreman, ‘Call the workers and pay them their wages, beginning with the last ones hired and going on to the first.’
마태복음 : 20 장 9 절 
“The workers who were hired about five in the afternoon came and each received a denarius.
마태복음 : 20 장 10 절 
So when those came who were hired first, they expected to receive more. But each one of them also received a denarius.
마태복음 : 20 장 11 절 
When they received it, they began to grumble against the landowner.
마태복음 : 20 장 12 절 
‘These who were hired last worked only one hour,’ they said, ‘and you have made them equal to us who have borne the burden of the work and the heat of the day.’
마태복음 : 20 장 13 절 
“But he answered one of them, ‘I am not being unfair to you, friend. Didn’t you agree to work for a denarius?
마태복음 : 20 장 14 절 
Take your pay and go. I want to give the one who was hired last the same as I gave you.
마태복음 : 20 장 15 절 
Don’t I have the right to do what I want with my own money? Or are you envious because I am generous?’
마태복음 : 20 장 16 절 
“So the last will be first, and the first will be last.”
마태복음 : 20 장 17 절

마태복음 : 20 장 19 절

마태복음 : 20 장 20 절

마태복음 : 20 장 21 절

마태복음 : 20 장 22 절

“We can,” they answered.
마태복음 : 20 장 23 절 
Jesus said to them, “You will indeed drink from my cup, but to sit at my right or left is not for me to grant. These places belong to those for whom they have been prepared by my Father.”
마태복음 : 20 장 24 절 
When the ten heard about this, they were indignant with the two brothers.
마태복음 : 20 장 25 절 
Jesus called them together and said, “You know that the rulers of the Gentiles lord it over them, and their high officials exercise authority over them.
마태복음 : 20 장 26 절 
Not so with you. Instead, whoever wants to become great among you must be your servant,
마태복음 : 20 장 27 절 
and whoever wants to be first must be your slave—
마태복음 : 20 장 28 절 
just as the Son of Man did not come to be served, but to serve, and to give his life as a ransom for many.”
마태복음 : 20 장 29 절 
As Jesus and his disciples were leaving Jericho, a large crowd followed him.
마태복음 : 20 장 30 절 
Two blind men were sitting by the roadside, and when they heard that Jesus was going by, they shouted, “Lord, Son of David, have mercy on us!”
마태복음 : 20 장 31 절 
The crowd rebuked them and told them to be quiet, but they shouted all the louder, “Lord, Son of David, have mercy on us!”
마태복음 : 20 장 32 절 
Jesus stopped and called them. “What do you want me to do for you?” he asked.
마태복음 : 20 장 33 절 
“Lord,” they answered, “we want our sight.”
마태복음 : 20 장 34 절 
Jesus had compassion on them and touched their eyes. Immediately they received their sight and followed him.
마태복음 : 21 장 1 절 
As they approached Jerusalem and came to Bethphage on the Mount of Olives, Jesus sent two disciples,
마태복음 : 21 장 2 절 
saying to them, “Go to the village ahead of you, and at once you will find a donkey tied there, with her colt by her. Untie them and bring them to me.
마태복음 : 21 장 3 절 
If anyone says anything to you, say that the Lord needs them, and he will send them right away.”
마태복음 : 21 장 4 절 
This took place to fulfill what was spoken through the prophet:
마태복음 : 21 장 5 절 
“Say to Daughter Zion,
‘See, your king comes to you,
gentle and riding on a donkey,
and on a colt, the foal of a donkey.’ ”
마태복음 : 21 장 6 절 
The disciples went and did as Jesus had instructed them.
마태복음 : 21 장 7 절 
They brought the donkey and the colt and placed their cloaks on them for Jesus to sit on.
마태복음 : 21 장 8 절 
A very large crowd spread their cloaks on the road, while others cut branches from the trees and spread them on the road.
마태복음 : 21 장 9 절 
The crowds that went ahead of him and those that followed shouted,
“Hosanna to the Son of David!”
“Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord!”
“Hosanna in the highest heaven!”
마태복음 : 21 장 10 절 
When Jesus entered Jerusalem, the whole city was stirred and asked, “Who is this?”
마태복음 : 21 장 11 절 
The crowds answered, “This is Jesus, the prophet from Nazareth in Galilee.”
마태복음 : 21 장 12 절 
Jesus entered the temple courts and drove out all who were buying and selling there. He overturned the tables of the money changers and the benches of those selling doves.
마태복음 : 21 장 13 절 
“It is written,” he said to them, “ ‘My house will be called a house of prayer,’ but you are making it ‘a den of robbers.’ ”
마태복음 : 21 장 14 절 
The blind and the lame came to him at the temple, and he healed them.
마태복음 : 21 장 15 절 
But when the chief priests and the teachers of the law saw the wonderful things he did and the children shouting in the temple courts, “Hosanna to the Son of David,” they were indignant.
마태복음 : 21 장 16 절 
“Do you hear what these children are saying?” they asked him.
“Yes,” replied Jesus, “have you never read,
“ ‘From the lips of children and infants
you, Lord, have called forth your praise’ ?”
마태복음 : 21 장 17 절 
And he left them and went out of the city to Bethany, where he spent the night.
마태복음 : 21 장 18 절 
Early in the morning, as Jesus was on his way back to the city, he was hungry.
마태복음 : 21 장 19 절 
Seeing a fig tree by the road, he went up to it but found nothing on it except leaves. Then he said to it, “May you never bear fruit again!” Immediately the tree withered.
마태복음 : 21 장 20 절 
When the disciples saw this, they were amazed. “How did the fig tree wither so quickly?” they asked.
마태복음 : 21 장 21 절 
Jesus replied, “Truly I tell you, if you have faith and do not doubt, not only can you do what was done to the fig tree, but also you can say to this mountain, ‘Go, throw yourself into the sea,’ and it will be done.
마태복음 : 21 장 22 절 
If you believe, you will receive whatever you ask for in prayer.”
마태복음 : 21 장 23 절 
Jesus entered the temple courts, and, while he was teaching, the chief priests and the elders of the people came to him. “By what authority are you doing these things?” they asked. “And who gave you this authority?”
마태복음 : 21 장 24 절 
Jesus replied, “I will also ask you one question. If you answer me, I will tell you by what authority I am doing these things.
마태복음 : 21 장 25 절 
John’s baptism—where did it come from? Was it from heaven, or of human origin?”
They discussed it among themselves and said, “If we say, ‘From heaven,’ he will ask, ‘Then why didn’t you believe him?’
마태복음 : 21 장 26 절 
But if we say, ‘Of human origin’—we are afraid of the people, for they all hold that John was a prophet.”
마태복음 : 21 장 27 절 
So they answered Jesus, “We don’t know.”
Then he said, “Neither will I tell you by what authority I am doing these things.
마태복음 : 21 장 28 절 
“What do you think? There was a man who had two sons. He went to the first and said, ‘Son, go and work today in the vineyard.’
마태복음 : 21 장 29 절 
“ ‘I will not,’ he answered, but later he changed his mind and went.
마태복음 : 21 장 30 절 
“Then the father went to the other son and said the same thing. He answered, ‘I will, sir,’ but he did not go.
마태복음 : 21 장 31 절 
“Which of the two did what his father wanted?”
“The first,” they answered.
Jesus said to them, “Truly I tell you, the tax collectors and the prostitutes are entering the kingdom of God ahead of you.
마태복음 : 21 장 32 절 
For John came to you to show you the way of righteousness, and you did not believe him, but the tax collectors and the prostitutes did. And even after you saw this, you did not repent and believe him.
마태복음 : 21 장 33 절 
“Listen to another parable: There was a landowner who planted a vineyard. He put a wall around it, dug a winepress in it and built a watchtower. Then he rented the vineyard to some farmers and moved to another place.
마태복음 : 21 장 34 절 
When the harvest time approached, he sent his servants to the tenants to collect his fruit.
마태복음 : 21 장 35 절 
“The tenants seized his servants; they beat one, killed another, and stoned a third.
마태복음 : 21 장 36 절 
Then he sent other servants to them, more than the first time, and the tenants treated them the same way.
마태복음 : 21 장 37 절 
Last of all, he sent his son to them. ‘They will respect my son,’ he said.
마태복음 : 21 장 38 절 
“But when the tenants saw the son, they said to each other, ‘This is the heir. Come, let’s kill him and take his inheritance.’
마태복음 : 21 장 39 절 
So they took him and threw him out of the vineyard and killed him.
마태복음 : 21 장 40 절 
“Therefore, when the owner of the vineyard comes, what will he do to those tenants?”
마태복음 : 21 장 41 절 
“He will bring those wretches to a wretched end,” they replied, “and he will rent the vineyard to other tenants, who will give him his share of the crop at harvest time.”
마태복음 : 21 장 42 절 
Jesus said to them, “Have you never read in the Scriptures:
“ ‘The stone the builders rejected
has become the cornerstone;
the Lord has done this,
and it is marvelous in our eyes’ ?
마태복음 : 21 장 43 절 
“Therefore I tell you that the kingdom of God will be taken away from you and given to a people who will produce its fruit.
마태복음 : 21 장 44 절 
Anyone who falls on this stone will be broken to pieces; anyone on whom it falls will be crushed.”
마태복음 : 21 장 45 절 
When the chief priests and the Pharisees heard Jesus’ parables, they knew he was talking about them.
마태복음 : 21 장 46 절 
They looked for a way to arrest him, but they were afraid of the crowd because the people held that he was a prophet.
마태복음 : 22 장 1 절 
Jesus spoke to them again in parables, saying:
마태복음 : 22 장 2 절 
“The kingdom of heaven is like a king who prepared a wedding banquet for his son.
마태복음 : 22 장 3 절 
He sent his servants to those who had been invited to the banquet to tell them to come, but they refused to come.
마태복음 : 22 장 4 절 
“Then he sent some more servants and said, ‘Tell those who have been invited that I have prepared my dinner: My oxen and fattened cattle have been butchered, and everything is ready. Come to the wedding banquet.’
마태복음 : 22 장 5 절 
“But they paid no attention and went off—one to his field, another to his business.
마태복음 : 22 장 6 절 
The rest seized his servants, mistreated them and killed them.
마태복음 : 22 장 7 절 
The king was enraged. He sent his army and destroyed those murderers and burned their city.
마태복음 : 22 장 8 절 
“Then he said to his servants, ‘The wedding banquet is ready, but those I invited did not deserve to come.
마태복음 : 22 장 9 절 
So go to the street corners and invite to the banquet anyone you find.’
마태복음 : 22 장 10 절 
So the servants went out into the streets and gathered all the people they could find, the bad as well as the good, and the wedding hall was filled with guests.
마태복음 : 22 장 11 절 
“But when the king came in to see the guests, he noticed a man there who was not wearing wedding clothes.
마태복음 : 22 장 12 절 
He asked, ‘How did you get in here without wedding clothes, friend?’ The man was speechless.
마태복음 : 22 장 13 절 
“Then the king told the attendants, ‘Tie him hand and foot, and throw him outside, into the darkness, where there will be weeping and gnashing of teeth.’
마태복음 : 22 장 14 절 
“For many are invited, but few are chosen.”
마태복음 : 22 장 15 절 
Then the Pharisees went out and laid plans to trap him in his words.
마태복음 : 22 장 16 절 
They sent their disciples to him along with the Herodians. “Teacher,” they said, “we know that you are a man of integrity and that you teach the way of God in accordance with the truth. You aren’t swayed by others, because you pay no attention to who they are.
마태복음 : 22 장 17 절 
Tell us then, what is your opinion? Is it right to pay the imperial tax to Caesar or not?”
마태복음 : 22 장 18 절 
But Jesus, knowing their evil intent, said, “You hypocrites, why are you trying to trap me?
마태복음 : 22 장 19 절 
Show me the coin used for paying the tax.” They brought him a denarius,
마태복음 : 22 장 20 절 
and he asked them, “Whose image is this? And whose inscription?”
마태복음 : 22 장 21 절 
“Caesar’s,” they replied.
Then he said to them, “So give back to Caesar what is Caesar’s, and to God what is God’s.”
마태복음 : 22 장 22 절 
When they heard this, they were amazed. So they left him and went away.
마태복음 : 22 장 23 절 
That same day the Sadducees, who say there is no resurrection, came to him with a question.
마태복음 : 22 장 24 절 
“Teacher,” they said, “Moses told us that if a man dies without having children, his brother must marry the widow and raise up offspring for him.
마태복음 : 22 장 25 절 
Now there were seven brothers among us. The first one married and died, and since he had no children, he left his wife to his brother.
마태복음 : 22 장 26 절 
The same thing happened to the second and third brother, right on down to the seventh.
마태복음 : 22 장 27 절 
Finally, the woman died.
마태복음 : 22 장 28 절 
Now then, at the resurrection, whose wife will she be of the seven, since all of them were married to her?”
마태복음 : 22 장 29 절 
Jesus replied, “You are in error because you do not know the Scriptures or the power of God.
마태복음 : 22 장 30 절 
At the resurrection people will neither marry nor be given in marriage; they will be like the angels in heaven.
마태복음 : 22 장 31 절 
But about the resurrection of the dead—have you not read what God said to you,
마태복음 : 22 장 32 절 
‘I am the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob’ ? He is not the God of the dead but of the living.”
마태복음 : 22 장 33 절 
When the crowds heard this, they were astonished at his teaching.
마태복음 : 22 장 34 절 
Hearing that Jesus had silenced the Sadducees, the Pharisees got together.
마태복음 : 22 장 35 절 
One of them, an expert in the law, tested him with this question:
마태복음 : 22 장 36 절 
“Teacher, which is the greatest commandment in the Law?”
마태복음 : 22 장 37 절 
Jesus replied: “ ‘Love the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind.’
마태복음 : 22 장 38 절 
This is the first and greatest commandment.
마태복음 : 22 장 39 절 
And the second is like it: ‘Love your neighbor as yourself.’
마태복음 : 22 장 40 절 
All the Law and the Prophets hang on these two commandments.”
마태복음 : 22 장 41 절 
While the Pharisees were gathered together, Jesus asked them,
마태복음 : 22 장 42 절 
“What do you think about the Messiah? Whose son is he?”
“The son of David,” they replied.
마태복음 : 22 장 43 절 
He said to them, “How is it then that David, speaking by the Spirit, calls him ‘Lord’? For he says,
마태복음 : 22 장 44 절 
“ ‘The Lord said to my Lord:
“Sit at my right hand
until I put your enemies
under your feet.” ’
마태복음 : 22 장 45 절 
If then David calls him ‘Lord,’ how can he be his son?”
마태복음 : 22 장 46 절 
No one could say a word in reply, and from that day on no one dared to ask him any more questions.
마태복음 : 23 장 1 절 
Then Jesus said to the crowds and to his disciples:
마태복음 : 23 장 2 절 
“The teachers of the law and the Pharisees sit in Moses’ seat.
마태복음 : 23 장 3 절 
So you must be careful to do everything they tell you. But do not do what they do, for they do not practice what they preach.
마태복음 : 23 장 4 절 
They tie up heavy, cumbersome loads and put them on other people’s shoulders, but they themselves are not willing to lift a finger to move them.
마태복음 : 23 장 5 절 
“Everything they do is done for people to see: They make their phylacteries wide and the tassels on their garments long;
마태복음 : 23 장 6 절 
they love the place of honor at banquets and the most important seats in the synagogues;
마태복음 : 23 장 7 절 
they love to be greeted with respect in the marketplaces and to be called ‘Rabbi’ by others.
마태복음 : 23 장 8 절 
“But you are not to be called ‘Rabbi,’ for you have one Teacher, and you are all brothers.
마태복음 : 23 장 9 절 
And do not call anyone on earth ‘father,’ for you have one Father, and he is in heaven.
마태복음 : 23 장 10 절 
Nor are you to be called instructors, for you have one Instructor, the Messiah.
마태복음 : 23 장 11 절 
The greatest among you will be your servant.
마태복음 : 23 장 12 절 
For those who exalt themselves will be humbled, and those who humble themselves will be exalted.
마태복음 : 23 장 13 절 
“Woe to you, teachers of the law and Pharisees, you hypocrites! You shut the door of the kingdom of heaven in people’s faces. You yourselves do not enter, nor will you let those enter who are trying to.
마태복음 : 23 장 14 절 
[14]
마태복음 : 23 장 15 절 
“Woe to you, teachers of the law and Pharisees, you hypocrites! You travel over land and sea to win a single convert, and when you have succeeded, you make them twice as much a child of hell as you are.
마태복음 : 23 장 16 절 
“Woe to you, blind guides! You say, ‘If anyone swears by the temple, it means nothing; but anyone who swears by the gold of the temple is bound by that oath.’
마태복음 : 23 장 17 절 
You blind fools! Which is greater: the gold, or the temple that makes the gold sacred?
마태복음 : 23 장 18 절 
You also say, ‘If anyone swears by the altar, it means nothing; but anyone who swears by the gift on the altar is bound by that oath.’
마태복음 : 23 장 19 절 
You blind men! Which is greater: the gift, or the altar that makes the gift sacred?
마태복음 : 23 장 20 절 
Therefore, anyone who swears by the altar swears by it and by everything on it.
마태복음 : 23 장 21 절 
And anyone who swears by the temple swears by it and by the one who dwells in it.
마태복음 : 23 장 22 절 
And anyone who swears by heaven swears by God’s throne and by the one who sits on it.
마태복음 : 23 장 23 절 
“Woe to you, teachers of the law and Pharisees, you hypocrites! You give a tenth of your spices—mint, dill and cumin. But you have neglected the more important matters of the law—justice, mercy and faithfulness. You should have practiced the latter, without neglecting the former.
마태복음 : 23 장 24 절 
You blind guides! You strain out a gnat but swallow a camel.
마태복음 : 23 장 25 절 
“Woe to you, teachers of the law and Pharisees, you hypocrites! You clean the outside of the cup and dish, but inside they are full of greed and self-indulgence.
마태복음 : 23 장 26 절 
Blind Pharisee! First clean the inside of the cup and dish, and then the outside also will be clean.
마태복음 : 23 장 27 절 
“Woe to you, teachers of the law and Pharisees, you hypocrites! You are like whitewashed tombs, which look beautiful on the outside but on the inside are full of the bones of the dead and everything unclean.
마태복음 : 23 장 28 절 
In the same way, on the outside you appear to people as righteous but on the inside you are full of hypocrisy and wickedness.
마태복음 : 23 장 29 절 
“Woe to you, teachers of the law and Pharisees, you hypocrites! You build tombs for the prophets and decorate the graves of the righteous.
마태복음 : 23 장 30 절 
And you say, ‘If we had lived in the days of our ancestors, we would not have taken part with them in shedding the blood of the prophets.’
마태복음 : 23 장 31 절 
So you testify against yourselves that you are the descendants of those who murdered the prophets.
마태복음 : 23 장 32 절 
Go ahead, then, and complete what your ancestors started!
마태복음 : 23 장 33 절 
“You snakes! You brood of vipers! How will you escape being condemned to hell?
마태복음 : 23 장 34 절 
Therefore I am sending you prophets and sages and teachers. Some of them you will kill and crucify; others you will flog in your synagogues and pursue from town to town.
마태복음 : 23 장 35 절 
And so upon you will come all the righteous blood that has been shed on earth, from the blood of righteous Abel to the blood of Zechariah son of Berekiah, whom you murdered between the temple and the altar.
마태복음 : 23 장 36 절 
Truly I tell you, all this will come on this generation.
마태복음 : 23 장 37 절 
“Jerusalem, Jerusalem, you who kill the prophets and stone those sent to you, how often I have longed to gather your children together, as a hen gathers her chicks under her wings, and you were not willing.
마태복음 : 23 장 38 절 
Look, your house is left to you desolate.
마태복음 : 23 장 39 절 
For I tell you, you will not see me again until you say, ‘Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord.’ ”
마태복음 : 24 장 1 절 
Jesus left the temple and was walking away when his disciples came up to him to call his attention to its buildings.
마태복음 : 24 장 2 절 
“Do you see all these things?” he asked. “Truly I tell you, not one stone here will be left on another; every one will be thrown down.”
마태복음 : 24 장 3 절 
As Jesus was sitting on the Mount of Olives, the disciples came to him privately. “Tell us,” they said, “when will this happen, and what will be the sign of your coming and of the end of the age?”
마태복음 : 24 장 4 절 
Jesus answered: “Watch out that no one deceives you.
마태복음 : 24 장 5 절 
For many will come in my name, claiming, ‘I am the Messiah,’ and will deceive many.
마태복음 : 24 장 6 절 
You will hear of wars and rumors of wars, but see to it that you are not alarmed. Such things must happen, but the end is still to come.
마태복음 : 24 장 7 절 
Nation will rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom. There will be famines and earthquakes in various places.
마태복음 : 24 장 8 절 
All these are the beginning of birth pains.
마태복음 : 24 장 9 절 
“Then you will be handed over to be persecuted and put to death, and you will be hated by all nations because of me.
마태복음 : 24 장 10 절 
At that time many will turn away from the faith and will betray and hate each other,
마태복음 : 24 장 11 절 
and many false prophets will appear and deceive many people.
마태복음 : 24 장 12 절 
Because of the increase of wickedness, the love of most will grow cold,
마태복음 : 24 장 13 절 
but the one who stands firm to the end will be saved.
마태복음 : 24 장 14 절 
And this gospel of the kingdom will be preached in the whole world as a testimony to all nations, and then the end will come.
마태복음 : 24 장 15 절 
“So when you see standing in the holy place ‘the abomination that causes desolation,’ spoken of through the prophet Daniel—let the reader understand—
마태복음 : 24 장 16 절 
then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains.
마태복음 : 24 장 17 절 
Let no one on the housetop go down to take anything out of the house.
마태복음 : 24 장 18 절 
Let no one in the field go back to get their cloak.
마태복음 : 24 장 19 절 
How dreadful it will be in those days for pregnant women and nursing mothers!
마태복음 : 24 장 20 절 
Pray that your flight will not take place in winter or on the Sabbath.
마태복음 : 24 장 21 절 
For then there will be great distress, unequaled from the beginning of the world until now—and never to be equaled again.
마태복음 : 24 장 22 절 
“If those days had not been cut short, no one would survive, but for the sake of the elect those days will be shortened.
마태복음 : 24 장 23 절 
At that time if anyone says to you, ‘Look, here is the Messiah!’ or, ‘There he is!’ do not believe it.
마태복음 : 24 장 24 절 
For false messiahs and false prophets will appear and perform great signs and wonders to deceive, if possible, even the elect.
마태복음 : 24 장 25 절 
See, I have told you ahead of time.
마태복음 : 24 장 26 절 
“So if anyone tells you, ‘There he is, out in the wilderness,’ do not go out; or, ‘Here he is, in the inner rooms,’ do not believe it.
마태복음 : 24 장 27 절 
For as lightning that comes from the east is visible even in the west, so will be the coming of the Son of Man.
마태복음 : 24 장 28 절 
Wherever there is a carcass, there the vultures will gather.
마태복음 : 24 장 29 절 
“Immediately after the distress of those days
“ ‘the sun will be darkened,
and the moon will not give its light;
the stars will fall from the sky,
and the heavenly bodies will be shaken.’
마태복음 : 24 장 30 절 
“Then will appear the sign of the Son of Man in heaven. And then all the peoples of the earth will mourn when they see the Son of Man coming on the clouds of heaven, with power and great glory.
마태복음 : 24 장 31 절 
And he will send his angels with a loud trumpet call, and they will gather his elect from the four winds, from one end of the heavens to the other.
마태복음 : 24 장 32 절 
“Now learn this lesson from the fig tree: As soon as its twigs get tender and its leaves come out, you know that summer is near.
마태복음 : 24 장 33 절 
Even so, when you see all these things, you know that it is near, right at the door.
마태복음 : 24 장 34 절 
Truly I tell you, this generation will certainly not pass away until all these things have happened.
마태복음 : 24 장 35 절 
Heaven and earth will pass away, but my words will never pass away.
마태복음 : 24 장 36 절 
“But about that day or hour no one knows, not even the angels in heaven, nor the Son, but only the Father.
마태복음 : 24 장 37 절 
As it was in the days of Noah, so it will be at the coming of the Son of Man.
마태복음 : 24 장 38 절 
For in the days before the flood, people were eating and drinking, marrying and giving in marriage, up to the day Noah entered the ark;
마태복음 : 24 장 39 절 
and they knew nothing about what would happen until the flood came and took them all away. That is how it will be at the coming of the Son of Man.
마태복음 : 24 장 40 절 
Two men will be in the field; one will be taken and the other left.
마태복음 : 24 장 41 절 
Two women will be grinding with a hand mill; one will be taken and the other left.
마태복음 : 24 장 42 절 
“Therefore keep watch, because you do not know on what day your Lord will come.
마태복음 : 24 장 43 절 
But understand this: If the owner of the house had known at what time of night the thief was coming, he would have kept watch and would not have let his house be broken into.
마태복음 : 24 장 44 절 
So you also must be ready, because the Son of Man will come at an hour when you do not expect him.
마태복음 : 24 장 45 절 
“Who then is the faithful and wise servant, whom the master has put in charge of the servants in his household to give them their food at the proper time?
마태복음 : 24 장 46 절 
It will be good for that servant whose master finds him doing so when he returns.
마태복음 : 24 장 47 절 
Truly I tell you, he will put him in charge of all his possessions.
마태복음 : 24 장 48 절 
But suppose that servant is wicked and says to himself, ‘My master is staying away a long time,’
마태복음 : 24 장 49 절 
and he then begins to beat his fellow servants and to eat and drink with drunkards.
마태복음 : 24 장 50 절 
The master of that servant will come on a day when he does not expect him and at an hour he is not aware of.
마태복음 : 24 장 51 절 
He will cut him to pieces and assign him a place with the hypocrites, where there will be weeping and gnashing of teeth.
마태복음 : 25 장 1 절 
“At that time the kingdom of heaven will be like ten virgins who took their lamps and went out to meet the bridegroom.
마태복음 : 25 장 2 절 
Five of them were foolish and five were wise.
마태복음 : 25 장 3 절 
The foolish ones took their lamps but did not take any oil with them.
마태복음 : 25 장 4 절 
The wise ones, however, took oil in jars along with their lamps.
마태복음 : 25 장 5 절 
The bridegroom was a long time in coming, and they all became drowsy and fell asleep.
마태복음 : 25 장 6 절 
“At midnight the cry rang out: ‘Here’s the bridegroom! Come out to meet him!’
마태복음 : 25 장 7 절 
“Then all the virgins woke up and trimmed their lamps.
마태복음 : 25 장 8 절 
The foolish ones said to the wise, ‘Give us some of your oil; our lamps are going out.’
마태복음 : 25 장 9 절 
“ ‘No,’ they replied, ‘there may not be enough for both us and you. Instead, go to those who sell oil and buy some for yourselves.’
마태복음 : 25 장 10 절 
“But while they were on their way to buy the oil, the bridegroom arrived. The virgins who were ready went in with him to the wedding banquet. And the door was shut.
마태복음 : 25 장 11 절 
“Later the others also came. ‘Lord, Lord,’ they said, ‘open the door for us!’
마태복음 : 25 장 12 절 
“But he replied, ‘Truly I tell you, I don’t know you.’
마태복음 : 25 장 13 절 
“Therefore keep watch, because you do not know the day or the hour.
마태복음 : 25 장 14 절 
“Again, it will be like a man going on a journey, who called his servants and entrusted his wealth to them.
마태복음 : 25 장 15 절 
To one he gave five bags of gold, to another two bags, and to another one bag, each according to his ability. Then he went on his journey.
마태복음 : 25 장 16 절 
The man who had received five bags of gold went at once and put his money to work and gained five bags more.
마태복음 : 25 장 17 절 
So also, the one with two bags of gold gained two more.
마태복음 : 25 장 18 절 
But the man who had received one bag went off, dug a hole in the ground and hid his master’s money.
마태복음 : 25 장 19 절 
“After a long time the master of those servants returned and settled accounts with them.
마태복음 : 25 장 20 절 
The man who had received five bags of gold brought the other five. ‘Master,’ he said, ‘you entrusted me with five bags of gold. See, I have gained five more.’
마태복음 : 25 장 21 절 
“His master replied, ‘Well done, good and faithful servant! You have been faithful with a few things; I will put you in charge of many things. Come and share your master’s happiness!’
마태복음 : 25 장 22 절 
“The man with two bags of gold also came. ‘Master,’ he said, ‘you entrusted me with two bags of gold; see, I have gained two more.’
마태복음 : 25 장 23 절 
“His master replied, ‘Well done, good and faithful servant! You have been faithful with a few things; I will put you in charge of many things. Come and share your master’s happiness!’
마태복음 : 25 장 24 절 
“Then the man who had received one bag of gold came. ‘Master,’ he said, ‘I knew that you are a hard man, harvesting where you have not sown and gathering where you have not scattered seed.
마태복음 : 25 장 25 절 
So I was afraid and went out and hid your gold in the ground. See, here is what belongs to you.’
마태복음 : 25 장 26 절 
“His master replied, ‘You wicked, lazy servant! So you knew that I harvest where I have not sown and gather where I have not scattered seed?
마태복음 : 25 장 27 절 
Well then, you should have put my money on deposit with the bankers, so that when I returned I would have received it back with interest.
마태복음 : 25 장 28 절 
“ ‘So take the bag of gold from him and give it to the one who has ten bags.
마태복음 : 25 장 29 절 
For whoever has will be given more, and they will have an abundance. Whoever does not have, even what they have will be taken from them.
마태복음 : 25 장 30 절 
And throw that worthless servant outside, into the darkness, where there will be weeping and gnashing of teeth.’
마태복음 : 25 장 31 절 
“When the Son of Man comes in his glory, and all the angels with him, he will sit on his glorious throne.
마태복음 : 25 장 32 절 
All the nations will be gathered before him, and he will separate the people one from another as a shepherd separates the sheep from the goats.
마태복음 : 25 장 33 절 
He will put the sheep on his right and the goats on his left.
마태복음 : 25 장 34 절 
“Then the King will say to those on his right, ‘Come, you who are blessed by my Father; take your inheritance, the kingdom prepared for you since the creation of the world.
마태복음 : 25 장 35 절 
For I was hungry and you gave me something to eat, I was thirsty and you gave me something to drink, I was a stranger and you invited me in,
마태복음 : 25 장 36 절 
I needed clothes and you clothed me, I was sick and you looked after me, I was in prison and you came to visit me.’
마태복음 : 25 장 37 절 
“Then the righteous will answer him, ‘Lord, when did we see you hungry and feed you, or thirsty and give you something to drink?
마태복음 : 25 장 38 절 
When did we see you a stranger and invite you in, or needing clothes and clothe you?
마태복음 : 25 장 39 절 
When did we see you sick or in prison and go to visit you?’
마태복음 : 25 장 40 절 
“The King will reply, ‘Truly I tell you, whatever you did for one of the least of these brothers and sisters of mine, you did for me.’
마태복음 : 25 장 41 절 
“Then he will say to those on his left, ‘Depart from me, you who are cursed, into the eternal fire prepared for the devil and his angels.
마태복음 : 25 장 42 절 
For I was hungry and you gave me nothing to eat, I was thirsty and you gave me nothing to drink,
마태복음 : 25 장 43 절 
I was a stranger and you did not invite me in, I needed clothes and you did not clothe me, I was sick and in prison and you did not look after me.’
마태복음 : 25 장 44 절 
“They also will answer, ‘Lord, when did we see you hungry or thirsty or a stranger or needing clothes or sick or in prison, and did not help you?’
마태복음 : 25 장 45 절 
“He will reply, ‘Truly I tell you, whatever you did not do for one of the least of these, you did not do for me.’
마태복음 : 25 장 46 절 
“Then they will go away to eternal punishment, but the righteous to eternal life.”
마태복음 : 26 장 1 절 
When Jesus had finished saying all these things, he said to his disciples,
마태복음 : 26 장 2 절 
“As you know, the Passover is two days away—and the Son of Man will be handed over to be crucified.”
마태복음 : 26 장 3 절 
Then the chief priests and the elders of the people assembled in the palace of the high priest, whose name was Caiaphas,
마태복음 : 26 장 4 절 
and they schemed to arrest Jesus secretly and kill him.
마태복음 : 26 장 5 절 
“But not during the festival,” they said, “or there may be a riot among the people.”
마태복음 : 26 장 6 절 
While Jesus was in Bethany in the home of Simon the Leper,
마태복음 : 26 장 7 절 
a woman came to him with an alabaster jar of very expensive perfume, which she poured on his head as he was reclining at the table.
마태복음 : 26 장 8 절 
When the disciples saw this, they were indignant. “Why this waste?” they asked.
마태복음 : 26 장 9 절 
“This perfume could have been sold at a high price and the money given to the poor.”
마태복음 : 26 장 10 절 
Aware of this, Jesus said to them, “Why are you bothering this woman? She has done a beautiful thing to me.
마태복음 : 26 장 11 절 
The poor you will always have with you, but you will not always have me.
마태복음 : 26 장 12 절 
When she poured this perfume on my body, she did it to prepare me for burial.
마태복음 : 26 장 13 절 
Truly I tell you, wherever this gospel is preached throughout the world, what she has done will also be told, in memory of her.”
마태복음 : 26 장 14 절 
Then one of the Twelve—the one called Judas Iscariot—went to the chief priests
마태복음 : 26 장 15 절 
and asked, “What are you willing to give me if I deliver him over to you?” So they counted out for him thirty pieces of silver.
마태복음 : 26 장 16 절 
From then on Judas watched for an opportunity to hand him over.
마태복음 : 26 장 17 절 
On the first day of the Festival of Unleavened Bread, the disciples came to Jesus and asked, “Where do you want us to make preparations for you to eat the Passover?”
마태복음 : 26 장 18 절 
He replied, “Go into the city to a certain man and tell him, ‘The Teacher says: My appointed time is near. I am going to celebrate the Passover with my disciples at your house.’ ”
마태복음 : 26 장 19 절 
So the disciples did as Jesus had directed them and prepared the Passover.
마태복음 : 26 장 20 절 
When evening came, Jesus was reclining at the table with the Twelve.
마태복음 : 26 장 21 절 
And while they were eating, he said, “Truly I tell you, one of you will betray me.”
마태복음 : 26 장 22 절 
They were very sad and began to say to him one after the other, “Surely you don’t mean me, Lord?”
마태복음 : 26 장 23 절 
Jesus replied, “The one who has dipped his hand into the bowl with me will betray me.
마태복음 : 26 장 24 절 
The Son of Man will go just as it is written about him. But woe to that man who betrays the Son of Man! It would be better for him if he had not been born.”
마태복음 : 26 장 25 절 
Then Judas, the one who would betray him, said, “Surely you don’t mean me, Rabbi?”
Jesus answered, “You have said so.”
마태복음 : 26 장 26 절 
While they were eating, Jesus took bread, and when he had given thanks, he broke it and gave it to his disciples, saying, “Take and eat; this is my body.”
마태복음 : 26 장 27 절 
Then he took a cup, and when he had given thanks, he gave it to them, saying, “Drink from it, all of you.
마태복음 : 26 장 28 절 
This is my blood of the covenant, which is poured out for many for the forgiveness of sins.
마태복음 : 26 장 29 절 
I tell you, I will not drink from this fruit of the vine from now on until that day when I drink it new with you in my Father’s kingdom.”
마태복음 : 26 장 30 절 
When they had sung a hymn, they went out to the Mount of Olives.
마태복음 : 26 장 31 절 
Then Jesus told them, “This very night you will all fall away on account of me, for it is written:
“ ‘I will strike the shepherd,
and the sheep of the flock will be scattered.’
마태복음 : 26 장 32 절 
But after I have risen, I will go ahead of you into Galilee.”
마태복음 : 26 장 33 절 
Peter replied, “Even if all fall away on account of you, I never will.”
마태복음 : 26 장 34 절 
“Truly I tell you,” Jesus answered, “this very night, before the rooster crows, you will disown me three times.”
마태복음 : 26 장 35 절 
But Peter declared, “Even if I have to die with you, I will never disown you.” And all the other disciples said the same.
마태복음 : 26 장 36 절 
Then Jesus went with his disciples to a place called Gethsemane, and he said to them, “Sit here while I go over there and pray.”
마태복음 : 26 장 37 절 
He took Peter and the two sons of Zebedee along with him, and he began to be sorrowful and troubled.
마태복음 : 26 장 38 절 
Then he said to them, “My soul is overwhelmed with sorrow to the point of death. Stay here and keep watch with me.”
마태복음 : 26 장 39 절 
Going a little farther, he fell with his face to the ground and prayed, “My Father, if it is possible, may this cup be taken from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will.”
마태복음 : 26 장 40 절 
Then he returned to his disciples and found them sleeping. “Couldn’t you men keep watch with me for one hour?” he asked Peter.
마태복음 : 26 장 41 절 
“Watch and pray so that you will not fall into temptation. The spirit is willing, but the flesh is weak.”
마태복음 : 26 장 42 절 
He went away a second time and prayed, “My Father, if it is not possible for this cup to be taken away unless I drink it, may your will be done.”
마태복음 : 26 장 43 절 
When he came back, he again found them sleeping, because their eyes were heavy.
마태복음 : 26 장 44 절 
So he left them and went away once more and prayed the third time, saying the same thing.
마태복음 : 26 장 45 절 
Then he returned to the disciples and said to them, “Are you still sleeping and resting? Look, the hour has come, and the Son of Man is delivered into the hands of sinners.
마태복음 : 26 장 46 절 
Rise! Let us go! Here comes my betrayer!”
마태복음 : 26 장 47 절 
While he was still speaking, Judas, one of the Twelve, arrived. With him was a large crowd armed with swords and clubs, sent from the chief priests and the elders of the people.
마태복음 : 26 장 48 절 
Now the betrayer had arranged a signal with them: “The one I kiss is the man; arrest him.”
마태복음 : 26 장 49 절 
Going at once to Jesus, Judas said, “Greetings, Rabbi!” and kissed him.
마태복음 : 26 장 50 절 
Jesus replied, “Do what you came for, friend.”
Then the men stepped forward, seized Jesus and arrested him.
마태복음 : 26 장 51 절 
With that, one of Jesus’ companions reached for his sword, drew it out and struck the servant of the high priest, cutting off his ear.
마태복음 : 26 장 52 절 
“Put your sword back in its place,” Jesus said to him, “for all who draw the sword will die by the sword.
마태복음 : 26 장 53 절 
Do you think I cannot call on my Father, and he will at once put at my disposal more than twelve legions of angels?
마태복음 : 26 장 54 절 
But how then would the Scriptures be fulfilled that say it must happen in this way?”
마태복음 : 26 장 55 절 
In that hour Jesus said to the crowd, “Am I leading a rebellion, that you have come out with swords and clubs to capture me? Every day I sat in the temple courts teaching, and you did not arrest me.
마태복음 : 26 장 56 절 
But this has all taken place that the writings of the prophets might be fulfilled.” Then all the disciples deserted him and fled.
마태복음 : 26 장 57 절 
Those who had arrested Jesus took him to Caiaphas the high priest, where the teachers of the law and the elders had assembled.
마태복음 : 26 장 58 절 
But Peter followed him at a distance, right up to the courtyard of the high priest. He entered and sat down with the guards to see the outcome.
마태복음 : 26 장 59 절 
The chief priests and the whole Sanhedrin were looking for false evidence against Jesus so that they could put him to death.
마태복음 : 26 장 60 절 
But they did not find any, though many false witnesses came forward.
Finally two came forward
마태복음 : 26 장 61 절 
and declared, “This fellow said, ‘I am able to destroy the temple of God and rebuild it in three days.’ ”
마태복음 : 26 장 62 절 
Then the high priest stood up and said to Jesus, “Are you not going to answer? What is this testimony that these men are bringing against you?”
마태복음 : 26 장 63 절 
But Jesus remained silent.
The high priest said to him, “I charge you under oath by the living God: Tell us if you are the Messiah, the Son of God.”
마태복음 : 26 장 64 절 
“You have said so,” Jesus replied. “But I say to all of you: From now on you will see the Son of Man sitting at the right hand of the Mighty One and coming on the clouds of heaven.”
마태복음 : 26 장 65 절 
Then the high priest tore his clothes and said, “He has spoken blasphemy! Why do we need any more witnesses? Look, now you have heard the blasphemy.
마태복음 : 26 장 66 절 
What do you think?”
“He is worthy of death,” they answered.
마태복음 : 26 장 67 절 
Then they spit in his face and struck him with their fists. Others slapped him
마태복음 : 26 장 68 절 
and said, “Prophesy to us, Messiah. Who hit you?”
마태복음 : 26 장 69 절 
Now Peter was sitting out in the courtyard, and a servant girl came to him. “You also were with Jesus of Galilee,” she said.
마태복음 : 26 장 70 절 
But he denied it before them all. “I don’t know what you’re talking about,” he said.
마태복음 : 26 장 71 절 
Then he went out to the gateway, where another servant girl saw him and said to the people there, “This fellow was with Jesus of Nazareth.”
마태복음 : 26 장 72 절 
He denied it again, with an oath: “I don’t know the man!”
마태복음 : 26 장 73 절 
After a little while, those standing there went up to Peter and said, “Surely you are one of them; your accent gives you away.”
마태복음 : 26 장 74 절 
Then he began to call down curses, and he swore to them, “I don’t know the man!”
Immediately a rooster crowed.
마태복음 : 26 장 75 절 
Then Peter remembered the word Jesus had spoken: “Before the rooster crows, you will disown me three times.” And he went outside and wept bitterly.
마태복음 : 27 장 1 절 
Early in the morning, all the chief priests and the elders of the people made their plans how to have Jesus executed.
마태복음 : 27 장 2 절 
So they bound him, led him away and handed him over to Pilate the governor.
마태복음 : 27 장 3 절 
When Judas, who had betrayed him, saw that Jesus was condemned, he was seized with remorse and returned the thirty pieces of silver to the chief priests and the elders.
마태복음 : 27 장 4 절 
“I have sinned,” he said, “for I have betrayed innocent blood.”
“What is that to us?” they replied. “That’s your responsibility.”
마태복음 : 27 장 5 절 
So Judas threw the money into the temple and left. Then he went away and hanged himself.
마태복음 : 27 장 6 절 
The chief priests picked up the coins and said, “It is against the law to put this into the treasury, since it is blood money.”
마태복음 : 27 장 7 절 
So they decided to use the money to buy the potter’s field as a burial place for foreigners.
마태복음 : 27 장 8 절 
That is why it has been called the Field of Blood to this day.
마태복음 : 27 장 9 절 
Then what was spoken by Jeremiah the prophet was fulfilled: “They took the thirty pieces of silver, the price set on him by the people of Israel,
마태복음 : 27 장 10 절 
and they used them to buy the potter’s field, as the Lord commanded me.”
마태복음 : 27 장 11 절 
Meanwhile Jesus stood before the governor, and the governor asked him, “Are you the king of the Jews?”
“You have said so,” Jesus replied.
마태복음 : 27 장 12 절 
When he was accused by the chief priests and the elders, he gave no answer.
마태복음 : 27 장 13 절 
Then Pilate asked him, “Don’t you hear the testimony they are bringing against you?”
마태복음 : 27 장 14 절 
But Jesus made no reply, not even to a single charge—to the great amazement of the governor.
마태복음 : 27 장 15 절 
Now it was the governor’s custom at the festival to release a prisoner chosen by the crowd.
마태복음 : 27 장 16 절 
At that time they had a well-known prisoner whose name was Jesus Barabbas.
마태복음 : 27 장 17 절 
So when the crowd had gathered, Pilate asked them, “Which one do you want me to release to you: Jesus Barabbas, or Jesus who is called the Messiah?”
마태복음 : 27 장 18 절 
For he knew it was out of self-interest that they had handed Jesus over to him.
마태복음 : 27 장 19 절 
While Pilate was sitting on the judge’s seat, his wife sent him this message: “Don’t have anything to do with that innocent man, for I have suffered a great deal today in a dream because of him.”
마태복음 : 27 장 20 절 
But the chief priests and the elders persuaded the crowd to ask for Barabbas and to have Jesus executed.
마태복음 : 27 장 21 절 
“Which of the two do you want me to release to you?” asked the governor.
“Barabbas,” they answered.
마태복음 : 27 장 22 절 
“What shall I do, then, with Jesus who is called the Messiah?” Pilate asked.
They all answered, “Crucify him!”
마태복음 : 27 장 23 절 
“Why? What crime has he committed?” asked Pilate.
But they shouted all the louder, “Crucify him!”
마태복음 : 27 장 24 절 
When Pilate saw that he was getting nowhere, but that instead an uproar was starting, he took water and washed his hands in front of the crowd. “I am innocent of this man’s blood,” he said. “It is your responsibility!”
마태복음 : 27 장 25 절 
All the people answered, “His blood is on us and on our children!”
마태복음 : 27 장 26 절 
Then he released Barabbas to them. But he had Jesus flogged, and handed him over to be crucified.
마태복음 : 27 장 27 절 
Then the governor’s soldiers took Jesus into the Praetorium and gathered the whole company of soldiers around him.
마태복음 : 27 장 28 절 
They stripped him and put a scarlet robe on him,
마태복음 : 27 장 29 절 
and then twisted together a crown of thorns and set it on his head. They put a staff in his right hand. Then they knelt in front of him and mocked him. “Hail, king of the Jews!” they said.
마태복음 : 27 장 30 절 
They spit on him, and took the staff and struck him on the head again and again.
마태복음 : 27 장 31 절 
After they had mocked him, they took off the robe and put his own clothes on him. Then they led him away to crucify him.
마태복음 : 27 장 32 절 
As they were going out, they met a man from Cyrene, named Simon, and they forced him to carry the cross.
마태복음 : 27 장 33 절 
They came to a place called Golgotha (which means “the place of the skull”).
마태복음 : 27 장 34 절 
There they offered Jesus wine to drink, mixed with gall; but after tasting it, he refused to drink it.
마태복음 : 27 장 35 절 
When they had crucified him, they divided up his clothes by casting lots.
마태복음 : 27 장 36 절 
And sitting down, they kept watch over him there.
마태복음 : 27 장 37 절 
Above his head they placed the written charge against him: this is jesus, the king of the jews.
마태복음 : 27 장 38 절 
Two rebels were crucified with him, one on his right and one on his left.
마태복음 : 27 장 39 절 
Those who passed by hurled insults at him, shaking their heads
마태복음 : 27 장 40 절 
and saying, “You who are going to destroy the temple and build it in three days, save yourself ! Come down from the cross, if you are the Son of God!”
마태복음 : 27 장 41 절 
In the same way the chief priests, the teachers of the law and the elders mocked him.
마태복음 : 27 장 42 절 
“He saved others,” they said, “but he can’t save himself ! He’s the king of Israel! Let him come down now from the cross, and we will believe in him.
마태복음 : 27 장 43 절 
He trusts in God. Let God rescue him now if he wants him, for he said, ‘I am the Son of God.’ ”
마태복음 : 27 장 44 절 
In the same way the rebels who were crucified with him also heaped insults on him.
마태복음 : 27 장 45 절 
From noon until three in the afternoon darkness came over all the land.
마태복음 : 27 장 46 절 
About three in the afternoon Jesus cried out in a loud voice, “Eli, Eli, lema sabachthani?” (which means “My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?”).
마태복음 : 27 장 47 절 
When some of those standing there heard this, they said, “He’s calling Elijah.”
마태복음 : 27 장 48 절 
Immediately one of them ran and got a sponge. He filled it with wine vinegar, put it on a staff, and offered it to Jesus to drink.
마태복음 : 27 장 49 절 
The rest said, “Now leave him alone. Let’s see if Elijah comes to save him.”
마태복음 : 27 장 50 절 
And when Jesus had cried out again in a loud voice, he gave up his spirit.
마태복음 : 27 장 51 절 
At that moment the curtain of the temple was torn in two from top to bottom. The earth shook, the rocks split
마태복음 : 27 장 52 절 
and the tombs broke open. The bodies of many holy people who had died were raised to life.
마태복음 : 27 장 53 절 
They came out of the tombs after Jesus’ resurrection and went into the holy city and appeared to many people.
마태복음 : 27 장 54 절 
When the centurion and those with him who were guarding Jesus saw the earthquake and all that had happened, they were terrified, and exclaimed, “Surely he was the Son of God!”
마태복음 : 27 장 55 절 
Many women were there, watching from a distance. They had followed Jesus from Galilee to care for his needs.
마태복음 : 27 장 56 절 
Among them were Mary Magdalene, Mary the mother of James and Joseph, and the mother of Zebedee’s sons.
마태복음 : 27 장 57 절 
As evening approached, there came a rich man from Arimathea, named Joseph, who had himself become a disciple of Jesus.
마태복음 : 27 장 58 절 
Going to Pilate, he asked for Jesus’ body, and Pilate ordered that it be given to him.
마태복음 : 27 장 59 절 
Joseph took the body, wrapped it in a clean linen cloth,
마태복음 : 27 장 60 절 
and placed it in his own new tomb that he had cut out of the rock. He rolled a big stone in front of the entrance to the tomb and went away.
마태복음 : 27 장 61 절 
Mary Magdalene and the other Mary were sitting there opposite the tomb.
마태복음 : 27 장 62 절 
The next day, the one after Preparation Day, the chief priests and the Pharisees went to Pilate.
마태복음 : 27 장 63 절 
“Sir,” they said, “we remember that while he was still alive that deceiver said, ‘After three days I will rise again.’
마태복음 : 27 장 64 절 
So give the order for the tomb to be made secure until the third day. Otherwise, his disciples may come and steal the body and tell the people that he has been raised from the dead. This last deception will be worse than the first.”
마태복음 : 27 장 65 절 
“Take a guard,” Pilate answered. “Go, make the tomb as secure as you know how.”
마태복음 : 27 장 66 절 
So they went and made the tomb secure by putting a seal on the stone and posting the guard.
마태복음 : 28 장 1 절 
After the Sabbath, at dawn on the first day of the week, Mary Magdalene and the other Mary went to look at the tomb.
마태복음 : 28 장 2 절 
There was a violent earthquake, for an angel of the Lord came down from heaven and, going to the tomb, rolled back the stone and sat on it.
마태복음 : 28 장 3 절 
His appearance was like lightning, and his clothes were white as snow.
마태복음 : 28 장 4 절 
The guards were so afraid of him that they shook and became like dead men.
마태복음 : 28 장 5 절 
The angel said to the women, “Do not be afraid, for I know that you are looking for Jesus, who was crucified.
마태복음 : 28 장 6 절 
He is not here; he has risen, just as he said. Come and see the place where he lay.
마태복음 : 28 장 7 절 
Then go quickly and tell his disciples: ‘He has risen from the dead and is going ahead of you into Galilee. There you will see him.’ Now I have told you.”
마태복음 : 28 장 8 절 
So the women hurried away from the tomb, afraid yet filled with joy, and ran to tell his disciples.
마태복음 : 28 장 9 절 
Suddenly Jesus met them. “Greetings,” he said. They came to him, clasped his feet and worshiped him.
마태복음 : 28 장 10 절 
Then Jesus said to them, “Do not be afraid. Go and tell my brothers to go to Galilee; there they will see me.”
마태복음 : 28 장 11 절 
While the women were on their way, some of the guards went into the city and reported to the chief priests everything that had happened.
마태복음 : 28 장 12 절 
When the chief priests had met with the elders and devised a plan, they gave the soldiers a large sum of money,
마태복음 : 28 장 13 절 
telling them, “You are to say, ‘His disciples came during the night and stole him away while we were asleep.’
마태복음 : 28 장 14 절 
If this report gets to the governor, we will satisfy him and keep you out of trouble.”
마태복음 : 28 장 15 절 
So the soldiers took the money and did as they were instructed. And this story has been widely circulated among the Jews to this very day.
마태복음 : 28 장 16 절 
Then the eleven disciples went to Galilee, to the mountain where Jesus had told them to go.
마태복음 : 28 장 17 절 
When they saw him, they worshiped him; but some doubted.
마태복음 : 28 장 18 절 
Then Jesus came to them and said, “All authority in heaven and on earth has been given to me.
마태복음 : 28 장 19 절 
Therefore go and make disciples of all nations, baptizing them in the name of the Father and of the Son and of the Holy Spirit,
마태복음 : 28 장 20 절 
and teaching them to obey everything I have commanded you. And surely I am with you always, to the very end of the age.”
